1)
Preparation for a New 7-Year Course
<Prayer> Today is November 6, 1966, the first Sabbath of this month, a new day that the Father desires. Father, there is no one to take responsibility for the sorrows of history. That sorrow is not the sorrow of heaven but the sorrow of the earth, yet the people on earth have not taken responsibility for that sorrow, so only You have had to bear it. We understand that despite the fact that the group that should fight against evil is the people of the earth, You alone have taken on that fight. 
Now, thinking that You are looking for someone who can take the place of that sorrow and can take on the fight You have been engaged in, we cannot help but call out to You with anxious hearts, thinking of how painful and sorrowful Your heart must be. Please allow us to acknowledge that we are Your sons and daughters, and as we think of a day as a year, a year as ten years or even a lifetime, let us recognize that the group that must manifest as the embodiment of that fight is gathered here today as the warriors of unification. We earnestly wish for this, Father. 
Thus, we have set out on a path of misery and have followed a sorrowful road. Because You have done so, we have come to understand that as those who have the heavenly relationship to follow in the footsteps of Your heart, it is an inevitable fact that we must participate in Your circumstances to live where You are. We know that we must take responsibility for the foundation of the ideology You desire, and we understand that this is the principle of the heavenly relationship. 
November 6, 1966 (Sun) Early morning, at the former headquarters church. 
8   Preparation for a New 7-Year Course
Therefore, grant us strong and courageous hearts as we seek to walk this path. 
May we not forget that You have been in a position where You could not even lament amidst the miserable course of history. We know well that You have always been such a Father since the beginning of history. Whenever we think of the circumstances in which You suppressed Your sorrow even in the past, and the painful circumstances of the Father who sought out a wishful individual in a historical era that could not recognize that heart, we sincerely thank You for allowing us to form a new gathering that can step forward to represent Your heart in such circumstances. 
We must strive with all our strength to fulfill that responsibility, and we must move with all our energy, pouring out all our sincerity, and we must not forget that our bodies must be offered as substantial sacrifices for the purpose You desire. 
Please do not let us forget that the way of the remaining cross is still calling us. 
On this new Sabbath, we cannot help but entrust this month to You, Father. We must struggle again. We must call out to You on this sorrowful path. We earnestly wish to be those who can strive towards heaven even at the peak of despair and long for Your heart. No matter what anyone says, we cannot sever the bond between You and us, and we know that no one’s circumstances can surpass Yours, so please allow our hearts to overflow with gratitude in our lives, and let us be Your sons and daughters who can call upon You with satisfaction and happiness. 
Today, Your scattered children have gathered in one place. We also believe that there are those who long for this Cheongpadong church, even if they could not be here. There are those who sincerely long for and admire this place, feeling that it is very precious. Please comfort them today. As a word of life, inspire them with new awareness and new stimulation. Thus, we earnestly wish for You to unleash the source of strength so that they can fight against this evil world. 
We do not want to call out to You from afar or discuss with You from a distance. Please allow us to understand that this is the ideology of the Unification Church and the integrity of the Unification Church. When we call You Father, may we realize that You are the Father who answers within our hearts, who becomes our shield in our lives, and who advises us. We must become children who can recognize this. If we find ourselves forgetting such things, may this time be one where we can once again repent before You, trembling in our hearts, and expose the appearance of being unfilial before You once more. 
Although the flow of history has caused us to form connections of twists and turns, we cannot help but express our gratitude once again for the efforts of the Father who has made it possible for the joy of sowing seeds. 
Father! Six years have passed since we set out on this 7-Year Course, and the day of facing the 7-Year milestone is imminent. When we reflect on this position once more, we must realize that we cannot stand before You with our own selves, nor can we offer anything to You. Father, we earnestly wish for You to have mercy on us, to become our friend, our Father, and our protector in our hearts, bodies, and lives. 
May the remaining days be filled with joy and accompany our lives, and may we be granted the joy and glory of being able to dwell with You in our heart lives. We earnestly ask that the glory of eternal ages be with You forever. We pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
<Words> When we compare our position when we set out on the 7-Year Course centered on the year 1960 with our current position after going through this 6-Year Course, we can clearly see that there have been unimaginable changes in our environment. 
This is something that you will well experience through your own faith life and by observing all the facts occurring around you. And considering all the facts happening nationwide right now, we must re-recognize how profound our mission is and how significant a responsibility we bear. 
You must also understand that after the first 7-Year Course ends, we must embark on the second 7-Year Course. 
Tasks to be Accomplished During the 7-Year Course
Through this 7-Year Course established in our Unification Church, we all know that a crucial question is whether we will become loyal subjects before God and true children. The titles of loyal subjects and true children cannot emerge from the ordinary positions of people who live comfortably. In other words, true loyal subjects and true children can only shine brightly and remain in history in extremely difficult and miserable environments. This is a fact that can be well understood by looking at the history of the past. 
As you walk this 7-Year Course, you must solely seek the path to your homeland, and you must bring the parents of your homeland. Furthermore, as those who have brought the parents of your homeland, you must establish the nation of your homeland. It is undoubtedly a fact that the course you must take is the 7-Year Course, feeling this mission deeply. 
Humanity lost its original nation due to the fall, and even after countless ages, it lost the true homeland that cannot be violated or invaded. This world of the homeland was ravaged by Satan, and history is about restoring this world of the homeland. We know that in the historical process, our ancestors disappeared amidst sorrowful twists and turns, or amidst weeping and despair. 
Born as descendants of the fall, carrying this historical sorrow, we cannot simply look at this evil world as it is in this era. As descendants who have inherited history, we must fulfill our responsibilities. However, we must examine how much we, as Unificationists, have stood in the place of replacing the history of the past and how much we have gone out in place of God, bearing the responsibility of the times. We cannot avoid reviewing this issue. Here, we see that we are at a stage where we must make new resolutions and new pledges both internally and externally. 
When you consider the Unification Church you believe in, the Unification Church you know, or the church and family you refer to as ours, we must ask whether it is demonstrating more than 100 percent value on this earth, and whether it holds such a distinguished position. If we say yes to this, then God cannot hesitate, and the Teacher Himself cannot hesitate either. You find yourselves in a position where you cannot affirm this either. This is the reality. Therefore, we must tighten our belts once more, eliminate all bad conditions in our environment, and gather our hearts with single-mindedness to make a resolution. This is the demand of the times and the task we must undertake as those who bear responsibility before this nation. 
God's Circumstances to Raise the Unification Group Again
Reflecting once more on 1966, ten months have already passed. In this year, we pledged before God to embark on the 4-Stage Boat Movement. We believe that the goals we set will be smoothly achieved. Some regional leaders and district leaders are overly confident about this, and there are groups worried about the number of members being gathered, but this is not because of your hard work or your efforts; it is because we have entered a time when such things are possible. Therefore, whenever we can have such thoughts, we cannot help but worry about how great our efforts have been over the past six years and how much our hard work has become a condition to repay before God. When we think about this, our efforts until now seem to be nothing. 
12   Preparation for a New 7-Year Course
When any individual in the world faces ruin in a day or an hour, it takes ten years or a lifetime to rebuild and restore that. When we consider this enormous historical purpose, that is, the great issue of providence, we must acknowledge that the efforts and hard work we have put into practice are exceedingly minimal. 
Now, we must be loyal only for heaven, and we must have a single-minded heart for heaven. The fact that tears and blood have been shed in every corner of the land, that it was not done alone, but that we embraced heaven on behalf of the nation and empathized with God's heart on behalf of all humanity, crying out and shedding tears, and also facing persecution and ridicule, will become seeds, and although the individuals who sowed them may have disappeared, the fruits will surely be harvested by God. We have reached the time for such a harvest. In other words, the environment has entered a stage where it can welcome us. 
This did not happen naturally. If we have sown, we must cultivate what we have sown ourselves. Despite having that responsibility, when we ask whether each of us has cultivated it in a position that God can be pleased with, we have not fulfilled our responsibilities. Both ourselves and others have failed in their responsibilities. The fact that we have produced such results, such changes in the environment, and such global circumstances is not something we have done. God has taken full responsibility for it. We must recognize that He has completed 95 percent of the responsibility. 
In this end time, God has conducted history through all historical eras, and the history beyond that...
You have acted with a poor sense of responsibility. You must understand that God has fulfilled 95 percent of the journey we must take, meaning He has taken on 100 percent of the responsibility. God is calling you again today. His hope is for thirty million to welcome Him so that He does not need to call you separately. However, since that is not the case, He must once again call someone from among this nation.

The person who can receive God's calling, that is, the one who can take on God's responsibility, is not someone who can be found in a day or two. Such a person must be able to accompany God's heart, drenched in hunger and blood, and this cannot be achieved in just a day or two. It requires a period of three to four years or more. Even knowing this well, you must understand God's difficult situation, where He has to select a responsible person from among the throngs of thirty million people, while leaving behind those who have worked hard.

You must feel and understand God's urgent heart, which requires that, despite knowing the wounds of your struggles and what your wounded selves look like, you must again turn back and present the wounded sons and daughters, that is, the diligent group for unification, to the thirty million people.

What is the most precious thing in the world? It is not gold or treasures, nor is it the world's fame or power. When asked what is the most precious thing between heaven and earth, it is oneself, precisely oneself.

However, when asked how to guarantee that oneself is precious, there is no answer. People do not possess what they should have, yet they want to be recognized as the highest value in front of the world. That is human nature. If we do not question how much others value the most precious "me" beyond the concepts of serving our nation and the world, we cannot make a new resolution and a new start.

As children of Korea, you know that you have a mission to align the Republic of Korea with God's will along with heavenly fortune. You have been running at the forefront for seven years, carrying that mission. When thinking about whom that was for, it was not for the nation, nor for the world, nor for any relative existence, but for the subject that is yourself. We often forget that it was for ourselves. Because I am infinitely precious and I am infinitely valuable, my individuality must become precious. To make my individuality precious, I must transcend my environment.

No matter how much gold and treasures one possesses, there must be an owner, and all people must recognize that value, and there must be an environment where it can be admired. Only then does that value become apparent. Therefore, you must realize that you are at a stage where you cannot sit idly by without thinking about the most precious "me."

Today, we are recalling past virtuous figures or great ancestors, but rather than thinking centered around them, we should think centered around ourselves, who must stand as historical fruits and era's pioneers. Valuing oneself as the most precious is an undeniable fact that all people feel in common. We must think about this once again.

Do you recognize your own value? How much value do you hold? Have you thought about this? If I am the only treasure in this universe, and I have become a true treasure, then that treasure will be longed for by God, by Jesus who has come and gone, and by countless saints who have come and gone throughout history. Even those who have established their own traditional thoughts in history will also long for it.

Not only in the past but also in the present, all people will long for it. They will envy that value. This will be true not only now but also in the future. However, until now, I did not know that I could be such a treasure.

But Jesus thought seriously in such a position. Even if He stood in a place where He was betrayed by everything in His earthly life, what did He center on, and how could He endure in such an environment? He knew His value, which could not be changed by anyone, more than anyone else, and He knew that He was the most precious treasure before the historical era. Anyone who is human, no matter what ideology they admire, must revere such a self, and because He possessed something that could not be attacked, He could not deny Himself even in a position where God was said to be unknown.

Then, when we look back at ourselves from the present point of view, am I indeed a precious being? How precious am I? When looking at a man, there are a wife, children, parents, and relatives around him. How precious is the existence of oneself, who connects relatives to the nation and the nation to the world?

Those who have lived until now, for example, those who have taken responsibility for their families, may be valuable in their families, but they may not be valuable in society. They may not be valuable in the face of their era. They may not have any value in the world. This is where the difference appears.

So what about Jesus? In His time, He could not be a valuable existence in front of His parents, siblings, and relatives, and in that society and era, He was completely denied, but from later generations, He gained value that could be welcomed. This was not because the people of that time were true, but because they did not recognize that value. The denial of Jesus implies a denial that contains the potential for acceptance. Thus, as time passes, what was denied naturally fades away, and only the value of truth remains. Jesus, who was denied in one era, emerged through a connection that could reclaim the historical era.

What is true value? People in the world try to succeed and become global figures. What will they do once they achieve that? They may boast of having global authority in their specialized fields, but what will they do with that? They may receive glory from all people in that field. However, there must be something that can be recognized 100 percent from all sides. This is impossible if one only possesses external, material things.

The teacher has seriously thought about this issue in the past. What is true value, true treasure that can monopolize the hearts and love of all people? True treasure is not something that can only be observed from a distance. It must be something that everyone can enter into, wear, and immerse themselves in. What kind of treasure is this? This treasure is not the external, material treasures of this world. It is the one and only love. Therefore, from that perspective, the path of virtue is to come out based on love.

Now, when we quietly observe the social realities we live in, can we establish such a value for ourselves? This is the problem. When we look at this world we live in, it cannot remain as it is. This era needs an absolute being who can judge in the court of justice with the law of righteousness from the best position. It is an era where evil prevails and captures good, where wicked people mock good people; even if we possess 100 percent true value, it is an era where we cannot reveal that value.

When we consider this, is it a good world or a bad world? It is a bad world. Is it a joyful world or a sad world? It is a sad world. Is it a happy world or an unhappy world? It is an unhappy world. It is a world filled with complaints and dissatisfaction, not a world of gratitude, satisfaction, and happiness. Everything is the opposite.

In such a desperate reality, what will supplement the responsible authority to conquer this? It is impossible with the ethics, morals, constitutions of nations, or any national system we have had until now. Although history has developed towards a new purpose along with historical changes, it has not yet solved this, which is why such results appear in the present world.

What will conquer this, and what will occupy this? This is an important question. To repel and eradicate this, we cannot have the current appearance. If humans possess the true nature, the treasure among treasures, they will not fall into the conditions of unhappiness that are widespread in the world. However, humans have fallen and lost the value of their true nature and their unique, precious self-concept, which is why religion has emerged as a supplement. Therefore, if we examine religion, most religions have the concept of the Messiah.

What is the Messiah? He is the one who brings forth a personality that can hold infinite value and infinite treasure for humanity. He is the one who governs heaven and earth and redefines the position of standards and measurements that cannot be exchanged for anything, and then comes to the human world. Therefore, what the Messiah brings is joy, goodness, and happiness. However, the world only has sadness, badness, and unhappiness. Goodness, joy, happiness, gratitude, and satisfaction belong to heaven, while badness, sadness, unhappiness, complaints, and dissatisfaction belong to Satan. You must clearly understand this. Where did the fall originally come from? It originated from complaints and dissatisfaction. Complaints and dissatisfaction led to unhappiness and sadness. This is the official path through which Satan invades humanity. Complaints are connected to unhappiness, and unhappiness is connected to sadness. Therefore, true virtue must have the content that can trample these down.

The essence of religion is gratitude. During the March 1st Movement, there was a significant incident in North Korea where a person who was a key figure was captured and tortured by Japanese officials, yet he shouted "Long live!" whether he died or lived. They urged him to die quickly. Despite being severely beaten and tortured, he continued to shout "Long live!" so much that they realized torturing him was futile and let him go.

In the same way, the essence of religion is gratitude. Therefore, if you were to mention the most important and urgent requirement to defend against Satan, it would be to be grateful. Next, it would be to be satisfied. Jesus passed these two tests smoothly, which is why God could not withhold the title of Messiah from Him. Although Jesus died on the cross, He demonstrated the authority of resurrection. Therefore, from the moment we receive the name of Jesus, a good, joyful world, a new historical day of hope, and a new morning will come.

However, how was Jesus seen in worldly terms? He was the representative of the unhappy, and if anyone were to speak of dissatisfaction, He could express it more than anyone else; if someone were to say something was bad, He could say it was worse than anyone else; and if someone were to say something was sad, He could be sadder than anyone else.

In the Garden of Gethsemane, Jesus prayed three times, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39) Here, the concept of overcoming was established. You who wish to find the infinite treasure of yourselves must want that value to be recognized. However, before standing in a position where that value is recognized, what must you do? You must have the authority to push aside everything around you while being in a buffer zone between heaven and Satan. If you do not have that authority, you cannot possess your own value, which is the fallen life. You must push this aside.

In that boundary, you must not stumble over any conditions. Everyone likes things related to happiness. Anyone, whether a disabled person or a dropout from society, likes happiness. However, no one in the world likes anything related to unhappiness.

What prevents me from moving in this sinful world? It is complaints and dissatisfaction. Such conditions of unhappiness envelop this society. You must understand that this is a necessary battleground we must conquer to transcend the world of death. Therefore, many religious people have fought their way out.

Because this fight is not yet over, this world does not brighten. It is because we have not been able to declare ourselves as victorious princes after winning this battle that we cannot bring forth the ideal lifestyle that God desires in this evil world. Therefore, we must recognize that history has continued the history of evil.

The standard of true family. You call those who enter the Unification Church "family," and how precious is that name? As I have said before, what does it mean to call someone family? This is not a term centered around you. It refers to the unique value, the infinite treasure that cannot be exchanged for the entire universe, centered around the only begotten Son of God, whom God loved, namely Jesus. 

God cannot help but love Him. If God's love is to be manifested, it can only be manifested through Him. If the path of God's victory is to be revealed, it can only be revealed through Him. If the standard of the beginning of heaven and earth is to be manifested, it can only be manifested through Him. Without Him, nothing of God can be revealed, for He is absolute. Only when centered around Him can we use the term family. The term family does not center around the current members of the Unification Church. It centers around Jesus in such a way.
A significant connection, centered on that personal aspect, is what we call family. When we look at Jesus, the older people would be His parents, and those similar to Him would be His brothers or sisters. You must understand that this is speaking about Jesus, who stands in a position of unique value, an infinite treasure.

So, could Jesus love His brother at that time? He could not love him even if He wanted to. That sorrow is the sorrow of Heaven. Even if there could be a connection between rich and poor, even if their circumstances aligned, even if their wishes and purposes matched... However, that did not happen, and it was an unfortunate situation for Jesus. If He became trapped in that misfortune and conquered by that complaint... But Jesus transcended that.

At that time, people should have stood as Jesus' brothers, parents, and relatives in order to finally establish a familial connection before Him. Considering that era, what if you stand in a similar position today? You must clearly understand that true value cannot be entered without being in a position of value like Jesus.

To avoid the invasion of Satan, first, you must not complain. From now on, think of Satan. If someone asks what kind of being Satan is, you should just answer that Satan is Satan, and if they ask if you've seen Satan, you should say that it exists but you don't really know it. That should not be the case. How does Satan invade us? What is the strategy by which Satan invades? You must know that when you have a heart of complaint about Heaven's will, the arrows of Satan come to you. Do members of the Unification Church complain a lot? They roll their eyes and say ridiculous things.

Your own value must be urgently cultivated by yourself. Of course, you should worry about what the world is like, but more than that, you must defend your own value and establish a policy for world salvation after achieving victory there. If you cannot cross your own boundary, no matter how loudly you shout, it will end there. Therefore, no matter how much you want to win, you cannot.

That is why you must not complain first. What was the first factor in the fall of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden? What did Satan use to tempt them? It was through complaint. Did God really say not to eat this? He sowed the seed of complaint. Adam and Eve were invaded by the arrows of complaint.

Looking at the current situation in Korea, everyone is poor, and life is difficult. That is because of the heavenly fortune. Otherwise, it would be abnormal. If there are people who are well-fed and living comfortably, they are people who have done unclean things. Such people will face a disastrous future. They will be destroyed. That is why the communists are rising up in Korea with a big club.

I believe that Korea is standing in a position to show a representative standard for establishing God's love and the laws of Heaven. Therefore, those who are living well and are satisfied in the current situation of Korea are all abnormal. So what is normal? It is to be hungry, to worry like a mountain, and if you live today, you should be filled with worries for tomorrow. That is an extremely unhappy fate, but if you overcome that, you will become extremely happy.

A compassionate Korean people. When I went to Jerusalem, I felt many things. When you go there, half of it is a desert area. When you see camels, you wonder if they can eat enough with such a large body in a semi-desert area without grass. Seeing that, I realized that Korea is a welfare among welfare.

The grapevines there are not even a handful. During the day, one-third of the leaves dry up under the sun's heat. The leaves become so wilted that you can't even tell if they are grapevines or some other vine. They all look like different vines. However, as hot as it is during the day, a lot of dew falls at night and dawn. That dew helps the plants regain vitality. Just like the plants growing in the land of Israel, the Jewish people also waited for the dawn and prayed in desperation before God in the quiet of that dawn.

Also, if you quietly look into their eyes, you can see something. It is something like emotion... The songs sung out of emotion are the greatest cries, and they are prayers filled with the heart. So, I felt that a new history began from here.

Thinking about this, the Republic of Korea has not yet become a wealthy country, but when you look at the clothes worn by young people and ladies, they are dressed better than any other people in the world. Moreover, even when compared to countries like England, two-thirds or more are wearing upper-class clothing. There is a saying that if you follow a well-dressed lady on the street, she will go into a shabby house made of straw. In terms of realistic circumstances, it is impossible to enjoy, yet they live a high-class and leisurely life. How do you think about this? This is a mystery about our people. If they had lived poorly for thousands of years, they would have been crushed and bent, but they have not.

Still, in Korea, the people have compassion for one another, and there is still humanity left. There is a kindness that cannot be found in any other people in the world. When you go to places like America, even among rich people, the father's possessions are separate from the son's. Even if the father and son eat together, the father pays for his own lunch, and the son pays for his own. However, Korean people, even among gangsters, when they go to a restaurant, they shout loudly that they will pay. They are a people who can do that, even if it is the end of the month. Seeing this, I felt that the Korean people are dignified and composed.

However, at this point, I think that the people of the Republic of Korea need to suffer a bit more. If I say such things, thirty million people might curse me. But I have already been cursed a lot, so it is okay to be cursed more. Even if I have been cursed to the point of dying by thirty million people, I have remained there with perseverance. Now, Heaven is asking for warriors who can stand firm in a place where all the people of the world are fleeing, to fight and conquer the enemy centered on a new ideology that the world cannot possess.

Thus, the Korean people are being tempered by suffering, by torment, and by hunger so that they can live and feel happiness anywhere in the world. I believe that when those who have been tempered spread out across the world and take offensive action, there will be no place that cannot be conquered. I like the Korean Tiger Corps and the Blue Dragon Corps. The soldiers of these units, when they go to Vietnam, do not think of dying without killing sixteen Viet Cong.

When we quietly observe our ladies, they are generally closer to Satan's side. The ladies might feel hurt by this. The other day, I heard on the radio about whether it is good or bad to complain about the price. When I heard that, I realized that women are the closest to being pawns of Satan. It is said that whether a household does well or not depends on the woman. Unification Church women must have their mouths unified, their ears unified, their eyes unified, and everything must be unified.

Those who complain are the first lineage of Satan. This must be realized. That is why I choose impressive words. What do we say about those who complain? They are the first lineage of Satan; those who harbor discontent are the second lineage, and the unhappy are the third lineage. Complaint, discontent, unhappiness—Satan controls all of these. There can be no joy, goodness, satisfaction, or happiness in front of a complaining person.
