He also lived by the principle of using cold water rather than hot water. In such a life, he came out while only longing for a heart that God could remember. Members of the Unification Church must live such a life. 

If Abraham had set out for the land God desired before God told him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, how pleased would God have been to see that? Similarly, if Noah had begun building the ark before receiving God's command, how pleased would God have been? 

Jacob, Moses, all were made to experience abnormal circumstances by being driven out by God to cultivate the heart of restoration. Likewise, the Israelite nation was also driven out of Egypt to enter the land of Canaan. They all carried out their tasks from the positions they were given. 

The path of restoration is a path we must inevitably take. God does not wish to carry out restoration providence through such national movements. He desires that it be done voluntarily. Therefore, to fulfill the heavenly will for the 30 million people, you must voluntarily undertake a great migration on behalf of the world. 

You must become someone who can say, "I will represent that nation. I will bury my bones in that land." However, in that regard, you are all failures, failures. You must be better than Adam, better than Noah, better than Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob. You must also be better than Moses and better than John the Baptist. Furthermore, you must be better than Jesus. The fruit that God has harvested after 6,000 years of labor must not be crushed and ruined in the historical age. However, since you are not doing so, it means you are not fulfilling your responsibilities in the new era. 

Then what should happen to that fruit? It must be recognized with a value that cannot be pushed out of any position. To be recognized with such value, God will gather all global satanic forces at once centered on the 7-year course of the Unification Church. During this period, you must come forward with a heart of filial piety and loyalty before God, yet you are acting as you please. 

The teacher has struggled to fulfill filial piety and loyalty before God until now. He has refrained from being in debt in the realm of the heart and has pioneered while being self-restrained and introspective. In that regard, the teacher has thought more than you. You must be more than that. The path we must take to represent the Korean nation will inevitably involve trials and tribulations. 

The path of restoration is a path you must take anyway. You must go instead of Adam, instead of Noah. To reach the position of victorious Adam, you must be liberated in front of all historical conditions of indemnity. And at the same time, you must surpass the standard of never receiving Satan's accusations. Otherwise, you cannot reach the position of victory. 

Restoration is centered on the heart. When you pray, of course, you should pray for the Unification Church to do well, but more than that, you should pray about how to overcome the path of restoration. 

In the path of restoration, you must first love the satanic world. Adam made mistakes in this connection, and Noah, Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, and the Israelite nation all failed in their restoration efforts. How can we restore this failure? A woman wearing a skirt should not live only for her household. Everything you do, whether eating or raising children, must be for the sake of tomorrow's nation. 

When the 7-year course ends, the teacher plans to establish a new church and move to this church. Until now, he has not been able to establish such a place, so he could not determine any systematic connection with God. However, now, with a period of 7 years, he has clearly established a place. When the teacher establishes a place, those who follow the Unification Church will also establish a place according to principle at that time. 

That is why the teacher has become someone without compassion and a ruthless person until then. He is someone who has even driven away his mother from the prison door. He is someone who has treated a mother shedding tears for her child in prison coldly. From a worldly perspective, the teacher is an unfilial son. A mother could not understand the son born on this earth who is doing God's work. In front of that standard, it is too shabby. That is why the teacher did that not as a son of his mother but as a son of God. 

The teacher's family has done the same. He is someone who has raised a beloved child through someone else's hands. Would the teacher have done that because he had no money? In the path of God's restoration, one cannot love their own first. God is someone who loves His own only after loving the satanic world. Therefore, you must set the condition of having loved the wicked offspring of the world's evil enemies, even if it means abandoning loving parents and beloved family. Only then can you love your own children without Satan's accusations. 

God, who dreams of a kingdom of love, cannot help but create a kingdom that is free from Satan's accusation. Similarly, since the Unification Church has come out with the ideal of an earthly kingdom, the teacher must walk that path. It must be done according to principle. Therefore, if you do not pass in the second 7-year course, it will be extended to the third. 

Just as God showed the path that His sons and daughters must take through Moses and Jacob in the path of restoration, the teacher must pave the way for you to walk. Do you understand? The 7-year course shows what the teacher's life has been like and what all the internal feelings the teacher has had toward you have been, and it paves the way for future generations to walk. 

This is the symbolic element, the figurative element, and the substantial element. The symbolic, figurative, and substantial do not separate; they form one body and pave the way while embracing the historical precedent, applying the legal conditions to countless descendants within the fallen realm for eternity. It applies to everyone. There is no forgiveness here. Therefore, it is principle. No matter what authority one has in the world, it does not exempt them from this. 

Until now, the teacher has been indifferent to blessed families, although he has blessed them. However, from now on, he plans to hold a general assembly of 36 families every year to address all these matters. In doing so, he aims to awaken those children who have forgotten how precious the blessing is. 

Blessed families must establish the foundation of the principled number, and even without the teacher, they must organize the Unification tribe going forward. In other words, the work of recording in the Book of Life has begun. The teacher reflects this before God, saying, "I offer the fruits of my life’s journey as a result of my struggles on earth before the Father, so please hand these over to me even if I have to overcome myself." You must understand that there is a responsibility to present this before God based on the principles of restoration. 

Because the time has come, I am telling you this. Do you understand? Therefore, from now on, your path will be very busy. That is why tears must come before meals, and repenting of your shame before God must come before putting on clothes. Thus, you must offer a burnt offering as a victorious priest before the Father in the reality of resurrection, passing through the historical age. 

Then what should the burnt offering be? Not a calf, not a child, but oneself. Abraham was willing to offer his child as a sacrifice, but God was grieved by that. God did not intend to carry out the work of restoration through his child. He intended to carry out the work of restoration through Abraham himself. The fact that God could not carry out the work of restoration through Abraham is God's sorrow. Likewise, in Adam's case, God could not carry out the work of restoration through Adam himself. God had no choice but to carry out the work of restoration through a child. 

Therefore, in the age of restoration, it is not about setting up one's child or calf. I must fight for myself. Otherwise, I cannot cross the peak of restoration. Do you understand? "Yes." Even if it means death, you must not forget that. I must give my all. If I am hit, I am hit; if I am despised, I am despised; if I go to prison, I go to prison. All sad matters must be my responsibility. I must become the very embodiment of the burnt offering. 

It is not the fall that future descendants could not offer their ancestors as burnt offerings. The fall is that Adam could not become the victorious prince by being the embodiment of the burnt offering. Thus, sadly, lambs are dying, and children are dying. We must become the offerings ourselves. We must pray that such things will never happen to our future descendants. The teacher is praying for that. You all must do the same. 

I must carry the path I must take in the 7-year course, and I must bear the responsibility I have before God in that heart. Rather than wishing for a comfortable and good environment, I must walk that path with tears, whether it rains or snows. Only by walking such a path in this world can I fully walk the path of restoration. You must definitely understand that this is how to conquer this world. Do you understand? "Yes." 

To go to the second 7-year course, I will ask you one thing. Raise your hand if you have decided to confidently go to the second 7-year course. Put your hands down. The time has come. To walk that path, the wealth you possess is not yours. You must be able to donate it as the wealth of the 30 million people. 

Your family must not be a family that only serves your own family; it must be a family that serves the 30 million people. Also, your body is not your own; it is a body that must go up as a burnt offering on behalf of the 30 million people. Therefore, to walk this path, you must first entrust your material possessions to God. The teacher has done the same. 

In the historical course of offerings, God first struck all things, then struck children, and then struck the parties involved. This is directly connected to the Unification Church today, and because it must be indemnified at once, all of the families that can symbolize the offerings must be offered before God. That is why I have placed my children in a position of sacrifice, making them starve and putting them in a pitiful situation. Thus, I must be able to receive a warning from God not to do that. God sent His Son into the satanic world, pushing Him toward the path of death, allowing Him to bleed at the hands of the enemy's spear and sword, all for the sake of carrying out the work of restoration. Therefore, to walk the path of restoration, you must offer even yourselves. 

The teacher will not shy away from anything to go beyond the 7-year course. If asked to pull a cart of dung, he would do it. 

You must walk the path of offerings and the path of atonement. This is a path that anyone must walk. Even the returning Lord must walk this path. You must become someone who can be recognized by Satan. The Unification Church is a place that walks such a path. It is not just for my own well-being; it is to save the nation. However, it is not just to save the nation and make it well. It is to unify the world through this nation being well. 

While people are pleased that Korea is receiving aid from the United States, the teacher is not pleased. Receiving aid means we acknowledge that we are a subdued nation.
is because it becomes. Our Unification Church is trying to save this society right now, but if we first incur debt from this society, we will perish. To save this society, we must incur debt. Do you understand what I mean? 
“Yes.” 
Have you offered symbolic, figurative, and substantial offerings? Until now, it has been the era of symbolic and figurative offerings. Because this has been centered around the Teacher, the world does not follow the Teacher. However, when it comes time to die, the Teacher is needed. When thirty million people die, the Unification Church's Teacher Moon will be needed. Furthermore, all the people of the world will need the Unification Church's Teacher Moon. This is an absolute principle. Just as Jesus said, “Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will never pass away” (Matthew 24:35), even if heaven and earth disappear, these words will remain. You are indebted to the Teacher. The Teacher has created a ladder and blessed the disciples, establishing the Ark of the Covenant for that. You just need to bring your bodies and be willing to burn with dissatisfaction. Who needs to burn? Your mothers and fathers, your children need to burn. This is the path of restoration through indemnity. 
Until now, children have been sacrificed to save their parents. Jesus died to save God. They were all caught in a trap. Therefore, at the end, mothers must worship their children, and fathers must worship their children. Because, providentially, children have stood in the position of offerings, children are Abel before their parents. Do you understand? You should not make excuses on the path of establishing such principles. 
Soon it will be 1967. We must prepare for that time from now on. After this seven-year course, you will not be able to enter the Teacher's house freely. Do you understand what I mean? There will come a time when you cannot enter freely. 
When you started on this path, you raised your hands and swore before the Father with determination in your hearts. 
I have to reflect again on what I have done since entering the Unification Church. Do you understand? “Yes.” 
The Second Seven-Year Course to Fight for the World 
After this seven-year course ends, we must start again. Until now, we have fought for Korea, but at that time, we must fight for the world. Therefore, the Teacher is planning to visit Japan and the United States before the end of March next year. 
At that time, the Teacher will test the members from Japan and the United States. Those people are not within the benefits of the seven-year course, so the question is how to bring them into that benefit. The Teacher is preparing to analyze their hearts through personal questions to grant them privileges. 
The Teacher wants the men and women of Korea who have received direct teachings from the Teacher to be scattered throughout the world, shedding tears and unfolding the will for the world. If the Korean people can be sent as missionaries to the world, the Teacher will be happy. So, how many people here can be sent as missionaries? 
The Teacher has chosen 120 holy sites in 40 countries around the world. We need to send missionaries who can take responsibility as national representatives for those 40 countries that have been chosen as holy sites, but the question is who to send. Raise your hands if you want to go. You should all be determined about such things. It is not just about going as missionaries and doing evangelism well. Even if you have to act like a beggar, leave behind the materials that you shed tears and sweat for that country and that people. If you cannot speak, then be mute. What good is it to speak? Can you not evangelize because you cannot speak? It is okay to be mute. 
With a heart that loves humanity and wishes for that nation to do well, pouring out all your sincerity, even if you have to be mute, that is precious. Only then can you become a nation with emotional subjectivity; otherwise, it cannot be done. Everyone, think about that. Here, from the association president... No one knows who will go. 
Take responsibility for the path of restoration 
The Teacher is a person who is crazy about the will. That is not the Teacher Moon's will. It is God's will. For the sake of the will, even if it means offering your children as sacrifices, that is something you can do. Conversely, if there is a heavenly command to offer parents as sacrifices, and if that is a heavenly will that can be recognized by all humanity and historical eras based on principles, then the Teacher believes that parents can also be offered as sacrifices. Do you understand what I mean? This is the Unification Church that has started with such a Teacher. That tradition and connection have not existed in historical eras. That is why I am mobilizing all of you to send everyone as missionaries abroad. 
As I mentioned earlier, there can be no more misery in the position where God must raise you as workers on behalf of this nation. Therefore, you who are present here today must not become miserable in such a position, and you must prepare from this evening with that determination. 
The Teacher has instructed to pray for 100 days from July 4 to October 14. What did he say to pray for? He said to pray with the Teacher's prison prayers, right? Do you understand why he said that? It was in the hope that you would become God's companions in the emotional aspect. It was to create the conditions to become companions of God. 
I have one request for you. There is a miserable crossroads ahead of you, so I ask that you maintain an unchanging attitude before God in the present and take responsibility for the path of restoration. You should not only be a Kim, but you should fulfill such responsibilities within the Kim clan. In other words, each of you should become someone who can fulfill such responsibilities within your own family and be someone who is not ashamed before the nation anywhere. 
<Prayer> My Father! I know that the Father I call has been so pitiful. I cannot help but realize that I must bear the pain given by You, looking at the standard by which humans can fall, and that I cannot leave behind a lament before the Father who is struggling and disappearing in the midst of such struggles. 
Father, the majority of humanity thinks that the Father, dressed in glory, rules the world and proclaims love for all people, wanting to embrace such a Father. That has been the desire of humanity until now. However, the Father that the members of the Unification Church hold onto is the Father who, in the midst of death, grinds His teeth while looking forward to a hopeful future, enduring day and night. The wish of the Unification Church members is to hold onto the Father’s hands, which have been wounded on the thorny path of countless hardships and sufferings, and shed painful tears. 
This long path of restoration, which cannot be repaid with billions of dollars and cannot be expressed with any words, has a historical sorrowful situation, so I earnestly hope and wish that the Father will allow us to accept the unfilial appearances that must repent a million times before the heart that says He will forget. 
As we stand before this seven-year course that started in 1960, as the time to surpass the seven-year crossroads approaches, may we become those who realize that the altar we are in must become a holy place of the holy sites, and may we repent and reorganize ourselves from this point today. 
No matter what anyone in the world says, it is not a matter of personal face or prestige. When the laws of the Father’s family are trampled upon and everything becomes cloudy before the Father’s will, we must become a group that knows how to go there, even if it means tearing our bodies and trampling our reputations. Please do not let us forget how much the Father has struggled to find such a group among the Unification group. 
As we look at the historical turning point where communism, which Satan moved during the seven-year crossroads centered on the 1960s, is now entering a stage of division and destruction like the setting sun, we must be aware of this. 
As the seven-year course ends, when we see the decisive standard that the changes in this world must be like this, there may have been Your disappointment, but the Father knows our hearts that are responsible for You, and we earnestly hope to be able to surpass this crossroads. 
For that work, You have worked hard, and I have struggled. When we see that the wish You had when You called and commanded us is now approaching, we must again put on the full armor and fulfill our responsibilities to God's heavenly mandate. Thus, starting as the perfect good itself, which cannot participate in evil, we hope to become individuals who can prepare for the welfare You desire to come to our door. To do that, we must become those who do not receive accusations from Satan. 
Father, I entrust my path to You, so please take responsibility. Now that we have entered November, may this month also be within Your will, and since we have responsibilities before this nation, Father, please do not withdraw Your hand of labor, and I earnestly hope that You will have mercy on us. 
Those who stand in opposition to God will be whipped by God, and those who cannot repay their debts of heart with tears will have to offer themselves as sacrifices for the conditions of indemnity before the nation or before all people. I earnestly ask that Your great love be with those who step forward to offer themselves as sacrifices. 
Please allow us to offer blessed content before You in this remaining year. May all the new resolutions we have made before You today remain in our hearts as a new explosive connection. I earnestly hope and wish that You will renew our bodies and minds so that we can leave something before Your remaining will of restoration. 
Please protect those who are fighting with the torch of the gospel in the desolate wilderness spread throughout the world. Father, I earnestly hope that You will sympathize with their loneliness. 
Just as You protected me during difficult times, just as You allowed the Unification group to reject all surrounding environments while fighting for six years, I earnestly hope that You will protect and encourage us so that we do not become weary. Thus, may we participate in the glorious position of the world and share in the blessings of the Father. 
Please do not let the lonely children spread throughout South Korea become weary, and may they not hesitate to charge toward the enemy's stronghold, the final destination, and may they not become those who add to the Father’s sorrow. 
May You lead our entire being according to Your will and allow us to discern all conditions of strength and environment to repay according to Your providential will. Please accept all of this today. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
2) 
To Become True Children 
There are many days in the world. After today comes tomorrow. There are countless days like this, but today we have gathered specifically to commemorate Children's Day. 
God wants to directly govern humanity 
It goes without saying that God created heaven and earth and wanted to enjoy joy. He also created Adam and Eve, and when they grew up to stand on the standard He desired, He wanted to bless them as a couple. Thus, He wanted to establish families centered around them, and through those families, establish tribes, nations, and the world. 
If Adam and Eve had not fallen and had fulfilled the purpose of blessing, that would have been the time to achieve both Adam and Eve's purpose and God's purpose of creation. Therefore, a new world of life would have begun from that time, but because Adam and Eve did not know that will and could not stand in the position God desired, the new world of life could not begin. In other words, both God's purpose of creation and Adam and Eve's purpose could not be fulfilled. Thus, a fallen family formed a fallen tribe, nation, and world. 
On November 12, 1966 (Saturday), at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was given in celebration of the 7th Children's Day (Lunar Calendar October 1) and has been compiled from <Seonghwa> No. 63 (February-March 1967). The title was added by the editor. 
God must conclude His original will, and because He must regain the original purpose lost through Adam and Eve, He has carried out the providence of salvation. However, the foundation upon which God has carried out the providence of salvation has been the realm of death and the dominion of evil. God lost the foundation upon which He could directly govern. 
Since God set Adam and Eve as the owners of love among all things created with love, if Adam and Eve and all things became one, then God could directly govern from that foundation. However, because humans, the center of all things, could not become one with God's love and fell into oneness with Satan, the foundation upon which God could directly govern was transferred to the world of Satan. 
This world, formed through the non-principled love connection of the world of Satan, is a world that has severed its relationship with God, so God had to restore this world according to the principles of creation. 
However, throughout history, God's hope has been to find children whom He can directly love, but He has not been able to find children whom He can directly love. There have only been those whom He could indirectly relate to, namely the ancestors who have come and gone. 
We can see that God has established our ancestors through an indirect historical process to save humans who cannot stand in a position to directly face God and remain within the realm of death, humans who are far from God. Representative figures such as Noah, Abraham, Moses, and John the Baptist are examples of this. We must understand that God has advanced the providence to reach a time when He can directly govern. 
God's providence of restoration and the resentment until now 
Although humanity has fallen, they cannot forsake God, so they had to descend to the position of a servant of servants. So what does it mean to be a servant of servants? It means there is no master. Fallen humanity must serve God from the position of a servant of servants. Satan was the archangel and a servant of God. Because humans were drawn before that servant, in order for humanity to return to God, they must establish a standard of having served faithfully before God from the position of a servant of servants. 
That is why God has led us out from the position of a servant of servants. However, even if God has placed us in the position of a servant of servants, we must establish the way of loyalty that can go forward with gratitude, sacrificing all our lives and possessions. Thus, we can rise from the position of a servant of servants to the position of a servant and then again from the position of a servant to the position of a son.
We know that we have risen to the position of direct children. 
Israel was established to set the standard of sonship beyond that of servants. Through the Messiah sent after 2,000 years of history, we are able to be grafted into the Messiah and, beyond the bond of sonship, finally rise to the position of direct children before God. However, because Jesus came to this earth and died on the cross, Christianity has woven a history of struggle in place of the sonship of Israel. 
So, what position has Christianity, which has gone through a history of struggle, been in? It has stood in the position of sonship. Therefore, it could not receive God's direct guidance. If Christianity had entered the position of direct children through the bond of sonship, God would have directly guided Christianity according to the laws of heart. If that had been the case, Christianity would have traversed the path of pioneers without countless sacrifices after Jesus. Thus, the entire world would have been absorbed into the Christian realm, and a foundation for complete victory would have been established, but this has not happened, and that has been God's sorrow until now. 
God could not fulfill His will and took Jesus away, leaving only the bond of sonship on earth. He promised to send Him back to this earth and has been guiding for 2,000 years to establish a foundation where the direct bond can be found centered on Christianity. 
So, what should Christians scattered around the world today do? They must desire to be directly grafted into the true children whom God loves. 
To become true children, they must not fail to desire this. 
The Messiah coming as True Parents
So, what qualifications will the Lord have when He comes in the historical end times? He will come with the qualifications of a parent. However, because Jesus could not take the position of a parent when He came to this earth, that is, He could not have a living foundation to comfort God representing all people while embracing Him in glory, the Messiah cannot come again as the Lord of glory. Therefore, the returning Messiah must first fulfill the duty of filial piety by inheriting the will that Jesus could not accomplish when He came to this earth, and only after establishing a foundation where He can comfort God by subjugating even Satan, can He qualify as True Parents. This is an overview of the restoration providence that God has been guiding until now. 
Before the Day of Children can come, the Day of Parents must come. Today, many people live with parents, but they do not have parents recognized by heaven and earth. There has been no Day of Parents that heaven could joyfully welcome, nor has there been a Day of Parents that the earth could joyfully celebrate as the happiest day. If such a Day of Parents had existed, that day would be a day that God rejoices in, a day that all people can enjoy, and a day that the entire universe can cheer for. 
On that day, God's love must be planted, and God must become one with His beloved son, and the heart that becomes one with all things must be cultivated there. However, due to human fall, such a day has not yet appeared in this universe. 
For this reason, God is restoring the Day of True Parents through the path of labor. Behind this lies the sorrowful heart of God and the historical grief accumulated over 6,000 years. Until these are resolved, the Day of Parents cannot possibly come. Because there must be a history of indemnity and restoration to resolve these, many prophets and saints have paid the price of blood. 
The law of heart centered on the family flows from parents to children. However, because this heart has not been planted, the effort to replant it is none other than the history of restoration. Here, the representative of men is the Messiah, and the representative of women is the Holy Spirit. 
In the beginning, the bride and groom were misaligned with the principles of heaven, and that must be organized and placed on the right track. The purpose for this remains, and thus God has been carrying out the providence of salvation. 
No matter how great a nation or ethnicity may be, without this providential standard, it is like a wandering star. No matter how long the history of this universe may be, it has continuously changed because a central traditional standard has not been established. In other words, it has not been a history that respects the bonds of tradition. 
Due to the fall of humanity, God scattered them and then unfolded the special providential will, gathering those who would be loyal before God. Thus, He established new families, tribes, and nations, and among these many nations, the nation that took on representative responsibility was the nation of Israel. Therefore, the nation of Israel became the central nation of the world. 
God's will for the nation of Israel and their disbelief
So, what must be present when we look for the essence of that central historical narrative? History should have developed centered on the standard of Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, but it has not, so there must be some standard centered on a criterion or ideology that can be re-presented. That standard must become the hope that Christianity longs for. In other words, it is the thought of the Messiah, and from the perspective of believers, it is the thought of the bride. 
So, what is the ultimate fruit of Christianity? It is not a Christian nation or a Christian world, but the highest realm of faith. A tree must have a trunk. No matter how many branches spread out in all directions, they spread from the trunk. No matter how long the branches may be, they cannot surpass the trunk. In the same way, if we compare all of humanity to a single tree, individual nations are like leaves, and the nation of Israel can be seen as the trunk, so if the trunk is thriving, it can become a normal tree. For this reason, God established Israel to form a nation and to shape the world. In other words, He must qualify Israel to connect the evil world to God's love. God intended for this to happen so that a new history could be realized. 
Centered on one purpose, God has been guiding for 6,000 years, and the end of that providence is now in this era. If the Day of True Parents had started 6,000 years ago and had formed nations and shaped the world normally, today this planet would have entered into God's dominion. However, the fact that this has not happened is the problem. For a single nation to emerge as the center among many nations, that nation must be loyal before God even when colliding with many other nations. 
The thought for the nation of Israel must be thorough, and at the same time, the thought for the world must also be thorough. Based on that thought, no matter how difficult the environment may be, even if entering the enemy's camp of historical foes, the heart longing for the New Israel must remain unchanged. Despite having such a heavy mission, because the nation of Israel could not carry on that tradition, it has flowed away, and the Second Israel, Christianity, has inherited that mission. 
So, what is the thought of the Messiah? It is the thought for the world. The center that can unify the world and unify families is True Parents. 
So, how does the fruit of Christianity manifest? Christianity is going through many trials and is moving toward the standard of the bride and groom. 
Even if this world is a dark world that has not formed a brilliant culture, a world of chaos, a desolate world, if there is only a connection to True Parents, this world is a kingdom of peace. Therefore, throughout history, many nations have focused their ideological concentration, mental concentration, and practical concentration on that being. God has externally led us toward a unified world and has internally guided us to connect to one Lord centered on religion. 
So, what trials must be endured until that parent comes? It is a mistaken thought to think that He will come riding on clouds in glory and commanding the heavens and the earth. According to the principles of heaven, if there are wounds, they must be shed. 
How is unity achieved?
So, who will remove those wounds? It must be the one who comes as True Parents representing humanity who will remove them. Since the children are in a position where they are wrapped in cloth, without removing that, the term liberation cannot exist. Without the unity of heaven and earth, that is, without the unity of the spiritual world and the earthly world, complete unity cannot be achieved. No matter how great a figure may come to unify the world with one thought, as long as the laws of heaven remain and God exists, it is nothing more than a delusion. 
Where is the cause of the failure of unity today? Everything is blocked. Before this can be broken down, unity cannot be achieved. If the gaps that are blocking from the foundation of heart, the foundation of mind, the practical foundation, and all existing worlds are not resolved, unity cannot be achieved. 
The gaps that must be resolved are not only on earth but are infinitely connected to the heavenly world. How will this gap be overcome? It is the responsibility of humanity, so humanity must resolve it. Therefore, for the Lord to come to this earth, He must engage in a fierce struggle with the blocked spiritual realm. The fact that a unified worldview is being established on this earth today is because a unified history is unfolding in the spiritual realm. Thus, the history of the spiritual realm is reflected on earth and unfolds into tangible reality. 
So, how is unity achieved? It is achieved by establishing the Day of True Parents on earth. The Day of True Parents is the day that decides victory between heaven and earth, the day that can be established as the day of victory that God has longed for, the day that can bear the historical fruit that humanity has hoped for, and the day that can find the lost owner of the universe. Without such a Day of Parents, the Day of Children cannot even be imagined. Therefore, the Unification Church has come forth to commemorate new days that do not exist on earth. 
We may simply think of today as the Day of Children, but we must understand that within that phrase lies the cries and calls of the ancestors who have labored on the crossroads of history. 
God has longed for the Day of Parents for 6,000 years.
God has longed for the Day of Parents to be established for 6,000 years. Originally, it was a day that the descendants of fallen humanity should have longed for, yet it is God, the Creator, who has longed for that day for 6,000 years. Since the day when the fallen history began, there have been many sorrowful and difficult events for God along the way, but amidst that, there was only one desire: the Day of Parents. 
By the arrival of that day, God can establish the true parents of humanity with whom He can be together, and He can declare, "You are the true parents of humanity." Thus, by coming forth with the name of the parents established by God, the standard of parental blessing is set. Here, by establishing true children, we can welcome the Day of Children on earth. When we think of this, it is truly lamentable that we, the members of the Unification Church, regard such a monumental day merely as one of the many commemorative days in the world. 
When people who love each other are in a position where they cannot possibly establish a bond by their own strength, if a new day is granted to them to establish that bond, there would be no one who longs for that day more than they do. This is human nature. 
The sun that rises and sets every day is always the same, but how much has God longed for that one special day among them? The day when God can forget all days and express Himself in joy before all creation is this day. 
When a parent loses a child, if there is a way to find them again, they will run without hesitation, even if it means facing death. When a parent loses their only child, realizing that child is so precious that they cannot be exchanged for their own life, they will not hesitate to cross mountains and seas to find that child. 
In this way, this day is a day of joy when we can open up the feelings that have been blocked and walk together on one path, and it is a day when the world can lay the foundation for unity. How much has God longed for today? Therefore, how could Satan remain still before God, who comes to find such children? He shoots arrows of fierce opposition. This is why the difficult storms of the world swirl around here. 
The Unification Church has gone through the harshest trials to welcome such a day. Without going through the bonds of sorrow, one cannot avoid the law of indemnity. 
While the fallen Adam and Eve bowed their heads to hide their shame, you who are walking the path of restoration must have the heart to bow before the Father, even as you go before God on the day of victory. 
We have gathered to find this bond. Some have come suffering from the waves of life, and others have come facing harsh environments. Our bodies are full of wounds. However, knowing that there is a God who has suffered greater wounds than ours, we cannot forget that we must comfort God. Herein lies God's compassion, and through this, we can establish a bond with God. 
To become true children
After overcoming the trials, a family will begin to form a tribe. So, when is the hardest time? The hardest time is when starting the seven-year course. At that time, a battle unfolds, and complete indemnity must be made one-on-one. On that foundation, Adam and Eve will establish a bond of love, and the world will come to a bright day. Thus, the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things have been established, forming these three stages. Humanity lost parents, lost children, and lost all things due to the fall. 
To establish the standard of indemnity for this, the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things had to be established, and among these, the most difficult day to establish was the Day of Children. This is because Adam and Eve could not become true children. 
So, how can one become a true child? One must be born from the same bloodline. To become a true child, one must fulfill filial piety before their parents. A filial child must navigate any difficult environment, be recognized by that environment, be recognized by the whole, and be recognized by their parents. God commanded Adam and Eve to govern all things, so Adam and Eve must receive recognition to govern all things. They must also be recognized as children who can take responsibility as the center of hope. And they must be in harmony with the heart of their parents. 
If there is a difference between the past, present, and future, one cannot be called a filial child. One cannot be called a loyal subject either. A filial child or loyal subject must not be corrupted. They must be able to represent the past, present, and future and be recognized from a position that transcends time and space centered on God's heart. 
So, when looking at history, who should the members of the Unification Church look to? They must look to God. And they should be able to say, "Aren't You such a Father?" Members of the Unification Church should look to the Teacher.
You must stand in a position where you can say, "The past was like this, the present is like this, and the future will be like this," and you must establish a standard that can represent God's past, present, and future, and can emotionally resonate with Him.

Since you are siblings born of one parent, your emotional experiences must be shared with one another. When your parents are sad, you should be sad together; when your parents are happy, you should be happy together; and even if you cannot labor alongside them, you should at least shed tears and realize your own shortcomings in order to receive forgiveness from your parents and remain within their protection.

You must have a humble heart that acknowledges that a being like me cannot stand before the standard of hope you have worked for; otherwise, you will become a lineage of Satan. The environment in which we can work hard to make amends, that is, within the realm of six conditions, is the last opportunity to celebrate the Day of Children.

If I go out centered on my heart, and if only the environment where my heart can resonate is prepared, the internal standard will be automatically established. We will see that the foundation where God can govern is becoming increasingly tangible before our eyes. However, while it is grateful that it is manifesting in reality, the question is what attitude I will take in front of that grateful reality. 

You must become members of the Unification Church who fulfill the duty of filial piety with the justification of children before a father whose face is clouded with worry, whose wrinkles have formed, and whose body bears countless marks from the arrows of enemies.

Are you living appropriately as a blessed family? We have been able to celebrate Parents' Day and Children's Day. It is through this process that blessed families have emerged. The Teacher has blessed the 36 families, 72 families, and 124 families. Blessings are not given to just anyone passing by; they are given to those who stand in a position representing heaven and earth.

To receive blessings, you must stand in a position where you have been recognized for fulfilling the duty of filial piety and possess the substantial value that can replace loyal martyrs. You must also become a personal representative who can return the authority of the earth and the authority of heaven to God, and be a man and a woman who can be recognized before heaven and earth.

You must have the confidence that there is no condition for Satan to accuse you, and even if you dislike it, you must advance to a position where you can say that God will bless you. Despite having received blessings based on such standards, I doubt how many people are living appropriately as blessed families.

You should live with a heart like that of a priest approaching the altar of atonement, worrying that your own wrongdoing might bring disaster upon the nation. However, we are not doing so. When the Teacher was imprisoned, God led enemies to the level of close friends. When we see this, we can understand how much God loves humanity.

When Jesus was crucified, He wanted to sweep away the entire opposing nation of Israel in one stroke, but because there were women weeping from afar, He was able to show compassion. When thinking of the nation of Israel, which has walked the path of misfortune until now, even if they are enemies, we cannot help but pray for their blessings.

Anyone can be grateful when someone gives them blessings and kindness. In a glorious position that all people can welcome, everyone can raise their hands in welcome. However, when one is in a lonely position, they do not welcome.

When the sound of flowing water becomes an object of comfort to me, nature finally has a connection with me, and when I have a heart that loves nature, the God who created that nature will love me. History is thus connected, and the twists and turns of history are unraveled from there, allowing enemies to become friends. When we think of this, we do not desire a cheap unification that anyone can welcome as we walk the path of unification today.

At the moment of desperation on Mount Calvary, the words of the thief on the right were words of comfort that could not be exchanged for the whole world. In those words, we can find the desire to rely on Jesus, to believe in Him, and to honor Him.

The year 1960, when the Teacher sent you out for evangelism and made rounds, remains very memorable. Nowadays, when I make rounds, many people line up to greet me, saying the Teacher is coming. However, I remember the lonely times when I stood in a cold wind, like a sentinel of the world of death or a flag of heaven pledging life, praying earnestly with my head bowed, and it is there that God creates connections with heaven and earth.

From this, we can understand that when in difficult positions, a heartfelt connection with God is formed. When Elijah was pursued and cried out that he was the only one left, God joined him in that heart. Because God was with him, a new authority of victory was given to Elijah.

The will of the parents is to elevate to the heavenly realm. Those who turn back from God due to suffering from their environment and living conditions, becoming mere passersby, are not worthy. No matter how terrifying the black clouds may bring a storm, you must become someone who remains until the end.

When I think of the many people who appeared as a focal point of hope before the path the Teacher walked, only to drift away like clouds, I sometimes wish they had not appeared at all. Moreover, when I have poured my heart and sincerity before God, and they turned back, that sorrow has lodged itself in my bones and cannot be removed. It is not because I hate such people, but because the damage caused to the nation is great. When I think of this, my frustration towards them arises in proportion to my love for the nation. However, I believe it is right to endure as long as there is no command from heaven.

God is not seeking just one family; He is seeking to find a nation through that family, and to find the world through that nation. Even if I am a citizen of the Republic of Korea, if I cannot love Korea but love the world and love heaven and earth, even if I am rejected in Korea, I will be welcomed when the global era and the heavenly era come.

Jesus lost the nation of Israel and the land of Israel, but He lived for the world that God desires and the heaven that God desires. He lived until His last breath. Therefore, although Israel perished, the world of filial piety will welcome Him, and the world of loyalty will welcome Him, so in the end, the world will move forward in His name.

You should regard being in the church as more precious than the treasures of your own family, even if you are like broken glass. Such a person can walk the path of loyalty and filial piety. This is someone who can enter heaven. In establishing this will, we must devote our sincerity to public matters.

You must love your brothers with your heart and love all things, becoming individuals who can move according to the will of the True Parents. So what is the will of those parents? It is not just to care for Korea, nor just for the world, but to elevate to the heavenly realm. In other words, through the connection of the True Parents, we must represent men and women and replace the high and the low. When that happens, everything that exists based on the principle of give-and-take will connect with the parents. Those True Parents came from God. Therefore, with a precious heart, we must repay God with precious results. Only then, when it expands to individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world, and appears as a common value before the whole, can we truly be called the sons and daughters of God.

**The Direction Blessed Families Should Take in the Future**
<Summary of the Message> Wherever members go, they should first seek a holy place, such as a holy site or a church, or at least establish such conditions.

Each of you must remember that you are not just individuals who remain as individuals. You must also stand in the position of your ancestors. The blessed family is established in a position like the Holy of Holies. God has sought blessed families for 6,000 years. He has come through countless prophets and Jesus.

Because God has labored to find you while enduring unspeakable hardships, each of you is an existence that cannot be exchanged for history. Therefore, you must shed tears and be grateful. You must not leave behind the fallen seed of Adam and Eve. You are in a position to establish laws for future generations. That is why you have been asked to endure hardships.

How much have you repaid for the blessings given by heaven? You must not think of public gatherings as personal matters. Personal matters must be sacrificed. The question is whether you can bear the fate of the world.

However, there is now nothing to establish before this nation. You must remain until victory is achieved. If you die before that, the work will go awry. Of course, each person has their own circumstances, but that is personal. The more you know God, the more you cannot lift your head.

Every time I receive letters from foreign members, I feel ashamed. I think about what responsibilities I have toward them. Blessed families do not come to the holy sites. Blessed families should be at the forefront on Sundays and public meeting days. One spouse must attend public gatherings. After seven years, families must be organized.

When crossing into the year 1967, everything must be settled. You must not pass your debts onto the Teacher. You must stand in a position to settle the three eras. As ancestors, you must pave the way for your descendants. To do this, you must sanctify yourselves morning and evening and sanctify your families.

Each family should make a white cushion. And prepare a clean place. So that you can sit on that cushion and have a time of devotion. Until the end of the seven-year course, I will take responsibility. I have no desire to bless again. When I see what is happening nationwide, I can tell that the time for the nation has come, but I find it pitiful when I look at blessed families. Therefore, even if it is through hardship, you must earn God's compassion.

I have placed even my body in a public position. To find what was lost to Satan, I must completely give up my own. Therefore, you must prepare mentally, practically, and environmentally.

Those who suffer first are the priests. Therefore, blessed families must first endure miserable experiences. Each person's path is busy. Now, I have commanded you to establish conditions for indemnity, but soon there will come a time when I will command you one-on-one.

Have you ever forgotten yourself and worked for the will? Have you ever worked from the position of a master rather than a servant? Have you ever felt shame at the barking of a dog in the neighborhood?

Those who are responsible cannot live comfortably. Do not incur debts. You must be of help to anyone because of yourself.

Now that we have entered the era of national salvation, you must evangelize your parents and siblings. In the seven-year course, basic families must be evaluated. There can be no exceptions here. You must save your enemies, even at the cost of sacrificing your sons and daughters.

Blessed families must raise their children in the position where the Teacher raised Seong Jin. You must love the Teacher's children more than your own.

The Teacher has not been able to say everything he wants to say.

**Our Attitude Towards Enemies**
Today is December 4, 1966, the first Sunday of the last month of this year. 

From the perspective of the will, until now, our Unification Church members have sworn with their lives and have rushed forward, even sacrificing everything for the sake of the will. Those days have passed for six years now.

**The Principle of Establishing Good**
During this time, you have had stories that you could not share openly with anyone, and you have carried burdens that you could not communicate with anyone. The Teacher knows this well.

What is the reason for standing in such a position? It is because you have vowed to cooperate in fulfilling the remaining will of restoration and to carry out the providence for this nation. Because of that vow, we have walked this path until now. Therefore, we have something to say before this nation. Moreover, we have much to say even before the 3 billion people of humanity. Furthermore, we have something to say even before God.

While pioneering this path, there have been many who have opposed us as enemies. However, in this current stage where the Unification Church has laid this foundation and is pioneering globally centered on Korea, should we regard those people as enemies? Should we take the position of resolving our personal grievances just because we are upset? We must reconsider this issue.

People tend to reflect on the past year on the last day of the year. During such times, people usually first think of the joyful events. They remember the unforgettable joys they experienced in certain months and times, and they feel a desire to share that joy with those who contributed to those events.

Humans do not boast about their joyful experiences themselves; rather, they want to boast about the people who participated in those joyful events. Conversely, when there are sad events, the greater the sadness, the more they want to eliminate that sadness.

Desiring to boast about the good and to eliminate the sad and painful is an inevitable principle in the historical process of establishing goodness. This principle is the same in religions that discern between good and evil to establish true goodness, and it is also universally applicable beyond any historical social environment through current social systems.

Until now, the Teacher has been aware that many enemies exist when trying to approach the world while dealing with personal, familial, and organizational lives centered on ideology. He has also understood that when walking the most miserable and despised path in life, there are times when the feelings of resentment and injustice may explode, but we must endure. This has served as a stimulus for the growth of the Unification Church and has also become a representation of sorrow.
Now we must completely eliminate our enemies from the world. This is the principle. If there are enemies of our parents, we must repay those enemies; if there are enemies of our tribe, we must repay those enemies; if there are enemies of our nation, we must repay those enemies. Furthermore, if there are enemies that harm the world, we must also repay those enemies. God, too, has a heart that cannot tolerate the burning anger in front of such enemies. We must understand that this is the heavenly principle. Regardless of whether one is a religious person or a member of society, regardless of status, this heavenly principle has governed and judged history.

No matter how sad, lonely, or unfair it may be, the members of our Unification Church must understand that while there is a law for those who walk the path of righteousness today, it is still a law that has been put on hold. No matter how much we want to curse, dislike, or repay our enemies, we cannot stand in a position where we can fully express our feelings and resist. This is the common situation of those who walk the path of righteousness.

We cannot repay our enemies even if we find ourselves in a fallen society, even if we are degraded, deprived, or exiled. Even when we are being pushed, we must quietly endure, and even in situations where our nation betrays us, we must quietly move forward. When we encounter environments that push us away in the flow of historical eras, we must silently be pushed away. You must understand that the path of religious people has been to trace this long history of sorrow.

The path of righteousness that we must quietly walk
You can remember the words Jesus spoke on the cross. "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing." (Luke 23:34) Jesus earnestly prayed before God. It is not that Jesus prayed this because he did not understand the situation. It is not because Jesus did not love his nation or was on the side of the nation's betrayers. It is not because he was in a position where he could not clarify God's heavenly law. It was solely because the time had not yet come. Even if Roman soldiers were stabbing him with their spears, it was not yet the time to repay those enemies, so Jesus had to embrace them until that time came, and we must not forget the sorrow that Jesus endured, knowing this.

The teacher declared a seven-year course centered around 1960. At that time, our church was in a period of trial. During that time, amidst the storm of criticism from society coming from all directions, when we faced an environment where we could not find even a glimmer of hope, the teacher did not command us to fight against the people.

"Have the smile of Esther. No matter what disdain you receive, have the attitude to accept it all. Even if you are sad, have the appearance of not being sad. Even if you feel wronged, have the attitude to forget that wrong. If you are furious and indignant, be prepared to forget your birth and endure." God encouraged us. When reflecting on these facts, you must understand that God had to come forth in this way today.

To subdue the enemy
If the teacher were to repay his enemies with personal feelings, there would be many who could strike them down in one blow, but the day to repay has not yet come. You must understand that because God is patiently looking forward to the day of hope, we too must endure. When we see the difficult realities of the Unification Church, we may want to release all the feelings of resentment we have towards our brothers, relatives, social organizations, nations, and the world, but you must understand that it is not the time to do so.

Reflecting on the heart of restoration, when we look at Cain and Abel before God, Cain was an enemy to Abel. When we look at Noah's family, everyone except Noah's family was an enemy to them. In the time of Abraham, everyone except Abraham was an enemy. 

In establishing the nation of Israel and going through Egypt, they suffered for over 400 years in the land of enemies. Although Jesus came to this earth and has been establishing the providential will for 2,000 years, it was also a world of enemies. Thus, God has had to enter the world of enemies and has the responsibility to subdue them, which is why He has endured until now.

This enemy is not a personal enemy. It is not merely a national enemy of a single Jewish state. It is also not an enemy on one side between democracy and communism. This enemy is the great enemy that destroys the world and the universe. The path of restoration is to look forward to the day when we can repay this enemy on the global stage.

Today, the members of our Unification Church are looking forward to the day when the will is fulfilled. You may resolve in your hearts that we must quickly fulfill the global will, the will pursued by all people, the will that heaven and earth both desire, but it is impossible to achieve that will centered solely on your individual selves. It is also impossible centered only on the Unification Church as a single organization. It is impossible centered only on the Korean nation. It is also impossible even if we unite the nations of Asia. We must solve the enormous problem of uniting the whole world and aligning the spiritual world in heaven. To fulfill this will, we must subdue the historical enemy, the global enemy, Satan, not by force but through natural subjugation. God has been pushing many religious people forward until now, looking at this tremendous responsibility.

Sacrifice 100 percent
What is the purpose of sacrificing individuals as offerings? It is not to repay personal enemies, but to sacrifice individuals to open the path for the nation. In other words, through the sacrifice of individuals, we aim to open the path for that nation. And sacrificing the nation means opening the path for the country in which that nation lives, and sacrificing the country means opening the path for the world. Because God has carried out the restoration providence in this way, it is an undeniable fact that the path of the Israelite nation, which has emerged with the victory rights under heaven's dominion, must be miserable.

God does not judge the whole because an individual stands on a victorious standard just because that individual has reached a victorious standard. God desires to reap a hundredfold or a thousandfold harvest from the sacrifice of one person, just as a grain of wheat falls to the ground and dies. Therefore, He says, "Sacrifice well, sacrifice well." He asks for a complete sacrifice without hesitation. When that happens, it will not just be a hundred percent like a grain of wheat, but even more will be harvested.

When God comes to each of you, He wants to place you as victors. So what must that individual do? They must overcome the enemy Satan that follows them. Does God know how to eliminate Satan? He leaves Satan behind.

There are family enemies that are greater than personal enemies, and there are national enemies that are greater than family enemies, and there are global enemies that are greater than national enemies, and there is the great enemy that has ruined heaven and earth, which is greater than the global enemy.

Therefore, even if an individual has repaid their family enemies well, the national enemies remain. Even if one has repaid their national enemies well, there is no way to stop the enemies that arise from betraying the nation. Even if the nation raises the banner of victory and proudly sings its rights and praises before the world, national victory alone cannot lead to eternal victory. Beyond national victory, national enemies remain, and even if one achieves national victory, it does not end there, as global enemies remain. Even if one achieves global victory, we must recognize that there are enemies who have deeply harmed heaven and earth and are wicked beings with the power of the entire universe. No matter how well one has repaid the lesser enemies, without repaying that enemy, one will find themselves in a position where they cannot achieve complete victory.

Even if one has repaid personal enemies, if they fail to win in the era of repaying family enemies, they will be struck first. And even if someone claims to have repaid family enemies, if they are defeated in the battlefield of repaying national enemies, they will be the first to be struck. When they are struck, it is all for naught. All beings involved cannot avoid shedding blood. And even if someone has repaid national enemies, if they fail to establish the authority of victory against national enemies and do not lay the foundation of goodwill, they will be opposed and struck by all people.

How loyal have you been before God?
Because this heavenly law remains, God says, "Endure! Endure!" Even if you enter the place of sacrifice on the cross, you must endure, and until the final moments when blood flows from your hands and feet and you are collapsing, you must endure. The sorrow of Jesus is the sorrow of God, and the difficulties of Jesus are the difficulties of God, and God would never welcome the death of His beloved only begotten Son, so why would God only tell us to endure? You must understand that meaning well.

Because the conditions to repay the global enemy were not established during Jesus' time, Jesus must come again. Therefore, you must understand that God has been running day and night, placing Christianity at the forefront and achieving miraculous developments. In the process, many people have been sacrificed. Many grieving souls have called for a future victorious nation, a victorious world. We have walked for a peaceful kingdom where heaven and earth can dwell and rest.

But have humans ever lived in such a homeland on any given day? Has Christianity ever pledged to reach such a world? Has there ever been a word from God that promised such a world? Because this has not happened, the final great battle remains. That battle must include everything. To establish that final day, the twists and turns of history have been colliding and clashing from the east, west, north, and south, and we have been struggling and returning.

From this perspective, when you quietly reflect on yourself, if I have been called before God and have lived for 6,000 years without dying, from the era of personal struggle to the era of family, nation, and global struggle, have I considered how loyal I have become before God? That is impossible.

You must understand that God has brought along these groups, who are easily swayed to believe today and betray tomorrow, and has led them to establish a new world centered on Christianity, enduring sacrifices of blood that you cannot even imagine.

People today think that living comfortably in an environment of advanced civilization is due to their own merits or the merits of their ancestors. However, that has been achieved through countless hardships behind history. Although it may seem that each is different and divided, we must recognize that there is a heaven with one purpose, and that is why any individual or any nation stands in such a position.

However, that person cannot remain in such a position forever, nor can that nation enjoy the glory of such a position indefinitely. If they forget the historical facts that led them to such a position, they must understand that the day of final judgment will call them.

Unification Church members must overcome the path of endurance
The teacher was prepared for the closest people to become enemies when starting the Unification Church. Personal enemies in daily life are easy to endure. Enemies that appear in personal situations are nothing. Who will take responsibility for repaying the enemies that appear while standing at the forefront of the world, carrying the fate of all humanity and the fate of heaven and earth? This is something to consider. Only the Messiah, who can govern heaven and earth, is the one who must do this. That is why the idea of the Messiah is necessary.

So what should the Messiah be like? They must know how to endure through the many twists and turns of history. They must be able to participate in the groans of history, go out to the places of great misfortune, and pass through the position of a true person who can digest it as their own.

If this is true, the Messiah who will come in the future cannot come in absolute glory. If they do, they are a false Messiah. The Messiah who comes must be a responsible person who can confront global enemies and win, without disappearing in the historical flow, even when faced with historical misfortune.

Today, the reason the teacher speaks like this is because there are many of our members in Japan, and among them, there seems to be lingering historical feelings between Korean expatriates and Japanese people. It seems that the yellow and blue colors have not yet faded. However, the question is how to eliminate the idea that this yellow is mine and that blue is yours, which has nothing to do with oneself.

The enemies that heaven must repay do not appear against individual countries like Japan or Korea. To strike this enemy, the entire world must unite. That is why Jesus said to all believers who follow him, "I am the vine; you are the branches." (John 15:5) In other words, he said we are one body.

That body should not be caught up in environments where individuals can rejoice, but should stand as a body that can bring joy to the world and to God. You must understand that God has hoped for this. Therefore, today's Unification Church is not a matter of relations between nations. No matter how much Japan strikes the global enemy, we must understand that the global enemy will return.

We must resolve the hearts of our enemies
Since Unification Church members have come to know God's will, they must walk the path of endurance for the final day that God desires. Even if there are moments where one must exchange their life, they must endure and overcome. The place of endurance is not a place where one betrays God and forgets God's hope and the overall responsibility that God desires. You must carry the will and quietly think about it, and go to the place where that will is established.

We are called bodies for the final day. December 1966, the time has come. If there are unresolved issues among Unification Church members, they must be resolved. We must die together if we must die, and we must be beaten together if we must be beaten, as we are of the same kind, and we must endure trials and hardships together.

We must unite with one another. Therefore, we must resolve the entanglements of individuals and families that have been formed around Satan. We must also burst open the entanglements that lie ahead of the coming nations, countries, and the world.

So how do we burst this open? To burst this open, it cannot be resolved by just my victory alone. First, we must unite families and relatives. To achieve national victory, we must unite tribes, and to achieve national victory, we must unite nations. Furthermore, to achieve global victory, we must unite countries. That is why a global religion must emerge quickly.
A religion that centers around the individual and prioritizes only oneself does not develop. A religion that, despite being particularly persecuted, collaborates between the individual and the whole to fight develops. Paul traveled around Asia Minor to evangelize, and in that sense, God raised him up. 

We should not seek revenge over trivial matters. We must resolve them. If there are issues among ourselves, we must resolve them among ourselves. Until now, established churches have regarded the Unification Church as an enemy. The teacher does not consider them enemies, but they treat us as such. We must tear down all walls, whether they are brick or concrete. If we want to bring all the members of the Unification Church today, we must open our hearts in exchange. 

They treat us like enemies, but we should not do the same. Regardless of who wins, in time, even enemies will fade away. Those who harbor enmity must let go of that sentiment. Those who carry enmity cannot enter the bright daylight. If that happens, let’s see who becomes the master. In the end, the bundles will be exchanged. Therefore, we must pledge for the final day that will come, the day we must repay the global enemies and the cosmic enemies. 

Our Attitude Towards Enemies
For this reason, we must prepare and move towards the dens of corruption and betrayal in every field. Until then, we must endure. This path is the normal way that heaven goes. Therefore, we must be entirely sacrificed for something greater, serve for something greater, and work for something greater. From that perspective, paving the way is the path of faith. 

People in the world say, “Ah! If you go to the Unification Church, you will only suffer.” However, the teacher does not think that way. Those who suffer for the teacher are fools. If that is the case, they should fail. If one is loyal only to the Unification Church, they should fail. If one is loyal only to the church, they should fail. Is God’s work a work for the church? No. It is a work for the world. The Unification Church must also serve the nation, the world, and heaven and earth. It is more important to serve heaven and earth than to serve one’s own church. Otherwise, when the time comes for heaven and earth to be established and for judgment to occur, that position will perish. 

When Jesus forgave his enemies on the cross, it was not because the enemies were good and deserved forgiveness. He knew that a greater enemy would come in the future and silently resolved to forgive his enemies for the day that heaven desires. 

God Has Not Yet Had a Joyful Day
God has not yet had a joyful day. Although God is the Creator who created all things, He has not had a joyful day that He can boast about throughout eternity. Why is that? When individuals led nations and brought about victories on a national level during the historical process, God was temporarily pleased. However, that joy did not become a joy that could consistently move heaven and earth and be praised highly, so that joy ended up being a temporary joy. Such joy is fleeting joy, a joy that can turn into sorrow tomorrow. 

God established Adam, but he failed. So, He established Noah and was pleased, but he also failed. He established Abraham and was pleased, but he too failed. He established Moses, but he also failed, which is why He sent Jesus. However, because even Jesus could not fulfill His purpose, God has not yet had a perfectly joyful day. Of course, He has had joy in saving individuals, but He has not had the supreme joy that He desires. 

So, what should you do? If you focus all your energy on the individual, God will bless that individual. If you focus your energy on the family, God will bless that family. What we do is precious because it is for something greater than the Unification Church. Also, because it is for something greater than ourselves, we are trying to set up a ladder to climb higher. Since God desires this, we must quickly welcome the day when we can repay the final enemy. If we do not repay the enemy and achieve victory, the Messiah cannot be born. 

Is the Son of God originally meant to be born in a world of enemies? Shouldn't the Messiah be born after clearing out all enemies and establishing a kingdom of peace? Until then, God must fight. However, God is not fighting for Himself. He is fighting to create the heaven where we can live. So, what must you do to enter heaven? Everyone must become one. 

When individuals gather to form a group, it is like a tribe that transcends families. Therefore, you are a unified tribe. The Unification Church is formed from individuals who have come together with a higher tribal connection than that of families. When trying to break this, one falls under the conditions of individual judgment, family judgment, and tribal judgment. 

God has told Christians and religious people to endure until the end. Thus, when the final judgment day comes, He has said to have the authority of victory that is not bound by any conditions. Only with such authority of victory can we freely enter before God. We must not forget that God has established the day of judgment to meet that day when we can respond to humanity without any obstacles in a free and equal position.

Therefore, you must clearly understand this. If there are those among the Unification Church members who are centered on themselves, they are a great enemy before the will. These are the spawn of Satan, worse than dogs or pigs. There are people who gather around themselves, praying and dreaming unrealistic dreams, and we must see how that will turn out. That is the fate of the times… It must be understood clearly, clearly. The essence of faith is wrong. Elevating oneself and treating others poorly is not the way of heaven. Unification Church members must reject this with their lives. Such groups are the internal enemies that determine victory or defeat on the stage where we must fight. 

They are asserting themselves before the nation that God desires. Those who regard those who are moving toward the original nation as enemies are Satan. You must understand this issue. It is not about repaying enemies; it is about not even coming into contact with such people. Each of you has a more urgent path to take. 

When you leave the church in the morning, you should look at the nation with concern, and beyond the nation's issues, look at the world's problems with concern, and advance with concern for God's will. We must worry about how we can quickly welcome the final day. Only then will it become a world of unification.
