Unification Church members should not engage in trivial conversations or fights when they meet, as they are meeting after 6,000 years. When we meet, we should talk about our church, our nation, and humanity. When members gather, they often talk about how well they are living, what they are dissatisfied with, and what is good. This should not be the case. Good and bad should not be centered on the individual. We should have the mindset to discern good and bad centered on a family that is greater than ourselves, and even more so, centered on a tribe, nation, world, and heaven and earth. 

What did Abel desire? He desired God's hope. What did Noah desire? Did he desire his family? His relatives? His nation? He desired a world figure who would appear in a higher era beyond the nation. 

When God blessed Abraham, saying, “Your descendants will be as numerous as the stars in the sky and the sand on the seashore,” Abraham had nothing at that time. However, in his heart, he seemed to have already conquered the world. The same goes for Moses. His purpose was not to live a luxurious life as the son of a princess in Pharaoh's palace. He knew that God would come to the nation of Israel, so he boldly resolved to sacrifice everything he had centered on the thought of Israel. Because he did so, he became a national leader who could guide the new Israel. 

To lead a nation, one must be able to overcome the trials that arise before that nation and repay the enemies. Only then can one become a responsible leader of that nation. 

From now on, when you Unification Church members meet and talk, you should not talk about yourselves, but rather exchange stories about our will, our church, our nation, and the world. Only then can we save this nation, save this world, fulfill God's will, and relieve God's sorrow. 

If you do not do that, you cannot escape the history of trials. Not only can you not escape, but your descendants also cannot escape. You must understand that this is the path of religion today, and the path that the Unification Church is taking, which is being persecuted among religions.

Why is the 7-Year Course Necessary?  
Spring, summer, autumn, and winter all follow the heavenly laws. It cannot deviate from the principles. It moves according to a certain orbit and must move according to some law.  
In an individual's life, one transitions from infancy to childhood, adulthood, and old age.  
The "I" who lived yesterday, the "I" who lives today, and the "I" who will live tomorrow are undoubtedly the same "I." But do you think there are no differences, gaps, or stages in that? You may not know, but when viewed from the perspective of life, some people may be in a fortune like spring during their childhood. Such individuals may have received benefits from their parents or special circumstances during their childhood. Others may start their youth in a spring fortune, while some may start their adulthood or old age in a spring fortune. The times may differ, but everyone is moving through fortunes like spring, summer, autumn, and winter.  
However, if many people all move in the same direction, it would be equal, but this is not the case. Some people move through spring, summer, autumn, and winter, while others move through winter, autumn, summer, and spring. Some are rising, while others are falling.  
Why does this happen? It is because the historical background of good and evil influences the aspects of life. What this means is that among your ancestors, there are both good and evil ancestors. The differences are vast, and they influence you.  
Good seeks to rise, while evil seeks to fall. When you do something and feel guilty about it, do you rise or fall? What about when things are good? You feel uplifted. This is the principle of heaven and earth. Evil people generally lower their heads and only look at the ground. Therefore, they shrink.  
Do thieves feel good when they steal? They do it while feeling anxious. However, when good things happen and exciting things occur, do their arms drop or rise? They rise. Their mouths open, and news spreads everywhere.  
This is not just a momentary occurrence; when things are good, both hands and feet keep rising. When things are bad, they keep falling. Moreover, good is released, while evil is bound. This is the principle of heaven and earth, so history does not move outside of that orbit. That state is moving in three-dimensional forms, colliding and breaking, and meeting again, moving in various forms.  
Many people enter this realm of operation, measuring their positions and only looking at that, declaring that this world is unfair, evil, and a miserable world, and thus many have meaninglessly given up their lives. Such people do not understand the laws of the universe.  
Humans in Cosmic Connections  
There is spring, summer, autumn, and winter even in a single day. Morning, noon, evening, and night are indeed spring, summer, autumn, and winter. The principles of heaven and earth are all like that. Throughout the four seasons of a year, everything that exists according to the laws of the earth revolving around the sun cannot avoid the benefits of that. This is an inevitable fact. You must understand this.  
You should see whether you are in a rising fortune or a falling fortune and whether you have inherited the merits of your ancestors or not. Some people may work three times harder or more than others and still not succeed. This is because they are in a falling fortune. They only rise after falling. At such times, if they put in effort, they fall faster. When a falling person puts in effort, they do not rise but fall even faster. Complete Restoration  
Complete restoration is something that everyone living on this earth hopes for.

God's Salvation Providence  
For each of us born as fallen descendants today, it is utterly impossible to restore ourselves completely. This is because we have fallen.  
That God, seeing humans who have fallen and could not even become servants of Satan, has compassion and raises humans to have hope to face God, placing them in the position of servants on heaven's side, and from there, leads those who are faithful to the position of servants.  
Thus, from the position of that servant, He brings them to the stage of adopting them as direct children.  
To be grafted means to be changed, referring to the adopted children becoming direct descendants. A person in the position of a second son must first judge the authority of Satan from the position of the first son before they can be changed to the position of the first son. This is how the game of grafting unfolds.  
Looking at the initial form of the beginning of history, since the world of Satan started first, it is in the same position as the first-born. In other words, until Jesus came, all of humanity in this world was the fallen descendants of Adam, and all of Adam's descendants are in the position of Jesus's brother.  
What kind of brother? A brother in the position of an adopted child. When we look at this, the first person to bear the responsibility of a direct son centered on God in this universe is Jesus.

**Qualifications to Celebrate Christmas**
Luke 2:1―
<Summary of the Message> Our church has celebrated Christmas on January 3, but this year we will celebrate it on this day according to the secular calendar. The day Jesus was born is a day that is unmatched for God. Because of this day, the way of hope was finally opened on earth. This day is the day that God has predestined throughout history, and for this day, God has made all preparations.

The Unwelcome Christmas
God placed hope in the Israelite people. However, their emotional standards did not align with God's hope. The fact that Jesus was laid in a manger is God's sorrow. This day, which should have been welcomed by all people, was not so because of the disbelief of the Israelite people, and this is God's sorrow.

From individuals to the nation of Israel, no one was prepared to welcome Jesus. Who prepared a room for the Messiah? Mary and Joseph also did not know the standard that God desired. Just by looking at the fact that Jesus was laid in a manger, we can see that Joseph's family could not fulfill their responsibility.

On December 25, 1966, at the former headquarters church.
* This message was organized from notes taken by former association president Yoo Hyowon.

Mary struggled in silence for ten months before giving birth to Jesus. It was regrettable that Mary herself could not stand in a position of external preparation. For Joseph, since Jesus was his stepson, as time passed and Jesus grew, Joseph began to have different feelings. Initially, he was in a position where he could not speak because of the angel's words, but after the birth of his own child, he treated Jesus even more so. Moreover, when his siblings hoped for the appearance of the elder brother, they mocked Jesus by asking why He did not go to Judea. Thus, we must understand that during Jesus' three years of public ministry, He had no place to stand from home to society.

We must understand how painful the life of Jesus was, who bore the responsibility for God, the Israelite people, all humanity, and future history. Yet until now, humans have not been able to celebrate this day as a day to relieve Jesus' resentment.

God, the Israelite people, and Jesus Himself should have rejoiced on the day of Jesus' birth. The day of Jesus' birth should have been a day of joy for the Israelite people and God. But was that day truly a day of joy?

Jesus, who should have been welcomed from the womb
Both God and Jesus lost this day. Therefore, to find this day again, God has been working to establish the Second Israel, which is the providential history of the past 2,000 years, and the day we seek is the day of the Second Coming.

Because the day of Jesus' birth did not become a day of joy for God, it is a grave matter to celebrate Christmas without knowing this meaning. If Jesus had been born as a prince of Rome, how glorious would His birth have been? Let alone being the only begotten Son of God. Yet, among the Israelite people, there was not a single person to welcome Him. How pitiful it was that God had to send the Magi from the East to testify to Jesus! The fact that a Gentile came and offered gifts to Jesus is a shame for the Israelite people and an insult to them.

Why was there no one in Israel as wise as the Magi? Jesus came to forgive the sins of 4,000 years of history. Yet, He was laid in a manger…. At that time, there was not a single person in Israel who could welcome the Messiah from the womb. If there had been even one such person, no matter how disabled, God could not have helped but love him. And Christianity would not have become a Gentile religion, nor would God's providence have shifted to Rome.

Anna knew the Messiah in the womb, so she should have become a servant of Mary and served the Messiah in the womb. However, she bore witness but could not serve. The Magi and the shepherds also only bore witness and then left.

Jesus should not have become a carpenter. Jesus was looking at the world through Israel. However, because He was not welcomed from home, He left home. That is why when He saw His mother and brothers who came to Him, He asked, "Who are My mother and My brothers?"

The Teacher has endured everything until now to relieve the resentment of God and Jesus. Because they did not believe in Jesus, the church leaders of that time had to go to hell. And the Israelite people had to live in hell on earth until the day of the Second Coming. Today, their independence is because the time has come for them to be forgiven. In the process of being forgiven, the symbol of Satan, Hitler, massacred six million Israelites.

The Israelite people should have prepared to welcome the Messiah from the time He was in the womb and should have welcomed Him upon His birth. What does it mean that pregnant Mary went to Bethlehem alone? If there had been more people to protect and accompany her than those who came to register in Bethlehem, could the Magi have welcomed Jesus?

The resentment of Jesus that must be resolved
Without clarifying the historical origins, we cannot solve contemporary issues. Who made the swaddling clothes that wrapped Jesus? Who washed His body and laid the baby Jesus somewhere? We must become those who understand this historical content and restore the resentment of Jesus.

Jesus, who left sorrow for God at His birth, and Jesus, who left resentment for God after His birth, could not tell anyone about this situation because He came with a heavenly mission. Therefore, Jesus lived looking at nature and appealing to it.

If there had been even one person who could comfort Jesus, He would not have been lonely. He had many things He wanted to eat. Such words are not in the Bible. It is a blessing that they are not. Those who believe in Jesus should not eat well or sleep well. Because Jesus did so. The Teacher finds it hard to say this.

However, Jesus could not forget Israel. After founding Israel, individual salvation was necessary, but only the thief on His right recognized Him. Therefore, this became the condition for God to remember the land, and because of that, the lifeline of Israel's salvation was not cut off.
Unexpectedly, just as a robber undertakes an unforeseen mission, an unexpected nation must arise to fulfill its mission at the end. Someone must come forth to walk the path of Jesus' death instead. Until now, it has been a period of indemnity, but the remaining days are not a period of indemnity.

**The Situation Regarding the Original Intention of Blessed Families**

**The Offering of Sincerity**
Everyone has hopes. To fulfill those hopes, it is human nature to want to prepare oneself at the place of sincerity and show oneself to the whole. This is not only true for humans but also for God. The reason humans have such a heart is that God, who created humanity, has it too. To leave some historical fruit in the world, or to achieve extraordinary results in that era to leave a model for future generations, and to remain as a foundation that descendants can emulate, one must go through the process of sincere effort. Behind every historical event, whether small or large, there is a process filled with sincerity that ordinary people cannot imagine, and only the results of such processes contribute historically and temporally. Therefore, today I will speak under the title of "The Offering of Sincerity." 

True sincerity means that we, living on this earth today, must recognize how many people have worked hard on the foundation of tearful sincerity to build a new cultural world. If there is a God who wishes to save the human world, that God must also prepare a foundation of even greater sincerity to establish that world. If one does not seek after preparing that, there is no way to save the world. Those who have walked this path in the past did not present a foundation of hope or a gospel of salvation to humanity. Knowing this fact, God has prepared a foundation of sincerity to carry out the providence to save humanity. 

For sincerity to be realized, the heart must be unified. In other words, one must have a single-hearted determination. There must not be two minds. From the beginning to the end, one must offer sincerity with a unified heart. Sincerity is not something that can be borrowed and returned. Therefore, if the beginning, process, or end changes in various forms, it cannot be sincerity. We must go with a single-hearted determination centered on a unified heart. However, if that heart is self-centered, sincerity cannot be realized. Sincerity must be offered not for oneself but for others, whether it be for family, society, or nation; only then does the noun "sincerity" come into existence. What is offered for oneself may remain for one's own lifetime, but it will flow away with oneself. The foundation of sincerity can only remain for others. The size of the results or connections of the sincerity offered is determined by the size of the counterpart. We often experience this fact in our daily lives. 

Therefore, you must remember that the requirements of sincerity are established not from a self-centered perspective but from a perspective that serves others. Thus, when a child offers sincerity for a parent, a wife for a husband, or a subject for their lord, the nouns of filial piety, loyalty, and devotion remain. This is because it is intertwined with history beyond the times, and it is inevitable that anyone would respect such standards and revere such connections. 

One must not be self-centered but must have a heart for others, and then one must also have God's heart. In other words, based on a foundation of love, one must have a single-hearted, unchanging heart for others for the noun "sincerity" to be established. To establish the noun of sincerity, one must continuously strive with a heart of love and single-hearted determination. 

And it must not end with having offered sincerity or loyalty. Continuous effort is required. However, effort alone is not enough. This is because unexpected misfortunes or counteractions may arise in serving the counterpart, and things do not always go as one wishes. Therefore, patience is also necessary along with effort. Moreover, patience alone is not enough. When something intolerable arises from within or around, one must have the courage to cut it off. For this, fighting is necessary, and one must go through the process of struggle. 

**The Standard of Sincerity in the History of Salvation**
Today, when observed objectively, human history can be said to be a history of struggle. However, it is not a blind history of struggle but a history of struggle with a consistent purpose. Therefore, behind that history of struggle are those who have offered sincerity. That sincerity is centered on their own ideas. When one invests all their sincerity, heart, and love into the counterpart world, the results of their efforts, patience, and struggles manifest as historical facts. From this, we can understand that the current realistic environment or all social systems exist because we need them, and behind them lies such connections. 

First, I must offer sincerity and become a person with sincerity. To do this, one must have a single-hearted determination, that is, a unified heart, and a heart that loves the counterpart deeply. When one has that heart of love and a single-hearted determination, that person can establish sincerity and achieve their purpose. Thus, to achieve a purpose, effort, patience, and struggle are necessary. Without going through this process, one cannot stand on the standard of a sincere heart and possess the value of sincerity correctly. This is evident not only in human history but also in the central figures established by God. 

So how has God worked to save fallen humanity, which has fallen into the world of death? If God had governed according to circumstances, saying "if it works, it works; if it doesn’t, it doesn’t," it would only conclude that He has been influenced by the distortions of social environments and the impacts of social systems. Such a history of God does not exist. This society has also come into being through the sincere connections behind it. Therefore, to save this world, Jesus could not help but stand in a position that is not influenced by social environments, centered on the foundation of sincerity behind it. 

So what determines the history of salvation? It is determined based on the standard of sincerity. When the sincerity of heaven is higher, even the society in the world of death can be absorbed before the sincerity of heaven. In other words, greater sincerity can absorb smaller sincerity. The original heart of humanity demands greater sincerity. And this is the standard of our conscience. Therefore, it is natural for humanity to desire greater sincerity and to move into the realm of greater sincerity rather than smaller sincerity. 

Everyone has the heart to become a patriot, a loyal subject, a filial child, or a virtuous woman. If there is a way to serve a certain society or nation, they hope to become such a person. Who would not love their own nation or country? Although there may be differences, the heart of love is the same. However, when any person representing a group, tribe, or nation offers sincerity, the majority cannot participate. For this reason, those who are appointed as representatives can realize the history of salvation by representing the ideological standards of that group, tribe, or nation and organizing the environment around that. 

So if God wishes to save the world, how should He act? He must offer sincerity. He must offer sincerity with a single heart, not two minds. There is a God who carries out the providence of salvation with a single-hearted determination that no one can invade, filling every corner of His heart. You must acknowledge this. 

Because of humanity's fall, this world has become the world of Satan, and Satan has violated humanity to the point where they cannot even stand as slaves. Although Satan has brought humanity down to the level of the lowest slaves, God has worked to save humanity. The descendants of the fall, born with the blood of enemies who cannot return to God, have a bloodline connection as children, but in reality, they have fallen into a position where they cannot be recognized as children or even as slaves. 

**God's Sincerity to Save Humanity and the Conditions Humanity Must Establish**
How does God save such humanity? It cannot be done casually. The sovereign of a nation must establish a standard that exceeds the love for his people. Also, in any organization, if God is to bring out the central figure of that organization as the one responsible for the providence of salvation and the liberator of humanity, he must possess a heart of sincerity that is more sincere than anyone who is loyal to that organization. 

To save humans who have fallen to the level of slaves of Satan as the servants of heaven, God's sincerity must exceed that of any sovereign or people who have offered sincerity within Satan and the satanic nation. If God's sincerity is lacking, He cannot save even one person. This is because Satan accuses Him. 

The God who created heaven and earth must stand as the highest standard before humanity and take a position of greater sincerity than anyone else. If He were to save someone from a position lower than Himself, it would be said that He has not completely saved them. 

If humanity in the world of Satan is left as they are, they cannot be established as the servants of the God who created heaven and earth. Therefore, to save humanity on this earth, God must offer a level of sincerity that exceeds that of Satan. And if there are people who are loyal to the sovereign nation of the satanic world, that person must stand in a position higher than the degree of loyalty they offer; otherwise, they cannot save humanity in the satanic world. Salvation means regaining what was lost. Therefore, the terms restoration and return arise here. For this, there has been a history of God's providence for salvation, like the history of Christianity. And you must acknowledge that behind God's providence for salvation lies a history of sincere struggle, a history of bloody patience and effort, and a history of tears of single-hearted determination. So how much sincerity must humanity offer to receive the benefits of God's providence? Humanity must also establish any conditions to stand before God, as Satan stands beside them accusing them every time they try to approach God.
Even when looking at the history of providence, this is true. How great must Noah's determination have been, having devoted his life to God's command for 120 years and embarking on that path? If there had been two hearts in him, he wouldn't have lasted even ten years. However, because he had a single-hearted determination that could pierce through his life and remain unchanged even if his life was tossed to and fro, and because he had a heart of compliance, a love that did not take God's command lightly, as well as a heart of patience and struggle, he was able to endure the long 120 years of reverse path. As a result, a relative condition was established to repay God's sincerity, and from there, history could make a new start.

Without the establishment of such conditions, the history of salvation providence cannot be built, and without establishing the history of salvation providence, a new historical beginning cannot occur, nor can providence be developed. This is the situation of God from the perspective of providence that you must understand.

After going through such a long history, the theory of salvation providence has remained on this earth. Humanity has gone through the era of servants in the Old Testament, the era of servants in the Old Testament, and the era of adopted children in the New Testament. Only after this can one advance to the original position of creation, where Adam and Eve were born with God's blood lineage in Eden.

To receive God, it should not be done individually, but the entire family must unite to receive Him. This was God's ideal in creating humanity. That is why Jesus came to this earth and said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride."

The stages of salvation providence and the measure of sincerity

Now, what we need to understand in the coming historical process is that to save those who have been connected to the world of Satan for 6,000 years, we must surpass the measure of sincerity that countless humanity in the world of Satan has put in. All our ancestors, including Noah, Abraham, and all others, went through this process. Therefore, if one does not love God more than their own children, they cannot go to heaven. Since we are in a bloodline relationship with Satan, if we wish to be restored, God requires us to pray. Thus, the Messiah is not coming to teach what is in the Old and New Testaments. If that were the case, we would not need such a Lord. The providential age will transition from the era of the servant of servants to the era of the servant, the era of the adopted child, the era of direct children, and finally to the era of the bride and bridegroom, that is, the parents' era.

In the Unification Church, there are also main currents and tributaries. The teacher has poured all his sincerity into leading the direction of the main current. The ideology of the Unification Church is the Way of Unification. The path of the Way is one that everyone must walk. If humanity had not fallen, they would have walked a smooth road. However, due to the fall, they ended up walking a miserable path. After the fall, this path had to be paved, and it had to start from the most rugged mountains. Therefore, the path of the Way began with prayers in the steep mountains.

Just as the Han River is formed by numerous streams, the path of the Way has been paved by many saints. The path of the Way began with pain and despair. To walk the path of the Way, one must pioneer the blocked paths. Thus, only through those who are more sincere can new paths be opened. The sacrificial offerings of blood...
After the era has passed, the era of commandments (this commandment is strict) will come, and after the era of commandments has passed, the era of faith will come.  
The 21-year course of the teacher is precisely the path that has been pioneered. Without establishing a path to restore the historical grievances that began with Adam, one cannot embark on the 21-year course. This vertical path of resurrection, growth, and completion must be realized horizontally, which is why we must walk the horizontal path of resurrection, growth, and completion. Those who have won in the first round can freely decide on the trial, and if they want to go, they can go, and if they want to stay, they can stay. Those who did not pass the first round cannot go even if they want to, but those who passed can participate in the trial in the third round. This is because it is a return process that extends into the first, second, and third rounds. Therefore, if you win in the first round, you can go to the second round, and if you win in the second round, you can go to the third round. If you have achieved a national victory in the first round, you will have the glory of national victory, and you will be able to bear significant responsibilities at the national level even in heaven. However, without extending the global responsibilities, you cannot enter a position of global responsibility.

In thinking this way, the leaders of the Unification Church must clearly understand. Even if the 36 families have fulfilled their responsibilities in the first round fight centered on Korea, they must again compete on the world stage. Therefore, you must understand how precious it is that you have participated in the first round fight of the seven-year course, fulfilling your responsibilities before God, shedding tears, and pouring out sweat and blood.

When did the words of the Unification Church begin to emerge? They began when the teacher was sixteen years old. This is not about discussing common sense or formulas for solving math problems. It is not about remembering some kind of style that a woman might want to show off, nor is it about finding a way to be remembered in the world as a man. You must remember your responsibilities as those who have taken on this fight with pride.

In this world where you were born, there are four great saints: Jesus, Confucius, Buddha, and Socrates. As we commemorate these saints, we come to long for the environments and lives behind their births, and thus the question of which country they were born in becomes significant.

The teacher has visited the land of Israel where Jesus was born. He has been to Bethlehem and Jerusalem, but those places were not considered the blessed land of Canaan flowing with milk and honey. There were only a few fields in the semi-desert area. Donkeys and camels were very noticeable there. And there were many olive trees. I felt that the climate there was not good because it is tropical.

Today, why do Christians from all over the world consider it the greatest happiness of their lives to pilgrimage to this Israel? It is because it is the place where Jesus was born. Confucius is great because the country was revitalized around his thoughts, and Chinese culture was created.

The same goes for Buddha. He was born a prince in the royal family but attained enlightenment through his own asceticism. He opened a path for all suffering people, which is why all those who were in pain remember him and simultaneously long for the country where he was born. This is why India has become an unforgettable country.

So, what should we, who are waiting for the saints, think about? We must think about their achievements. When we think about their achievements, we will think about the environments that contributed to those achievements, and then we cannot help but think about the country where the saints were born. Therefore, even if the country where a global saint was born is a desolate and devastated land, there are still people who can visit that land. You cannot deny this.

In any era of history, the sovereigns who boasted of their culture and power in their countries have all flowed away, leaving only a page in history. However, if there is a saint who has laid the ideological foundation through experience and has created a global culture, whether it is India, Israel, or Greece, we cannot help but long for such countries. Even if that country has perished, we want to trace the traces left by that saint, recall the state of the time when he lived, and connect with the culture and emotional experiences of that era.

The ideology of the Unification Church can only arise once in the providence of God's restoration. It cannot happen again. Also, from an external perspective, we are in an unprecedented historical moment. How tremendous is this fact? The current reality of the Korean people is so tragic. It is a nation that bears an unspeakable heavy responsibility and is in a position to be pitied by various nations of the world. However, even in such an environment, the cultural foundation and ideological framework that can establish a new world will emerge in the world through the movements of the Unification Church. If we dedicate ourselves to that, we cannot deny that the unfortunate position we are in today becomes a place of struggle for historical happiness.

So, do you think the ideology of the Unification Church is beyond the standards set by Jesus, or beyond the standards set by Buddha? You must have a new recognition of the headquarters church, a new recognition of the Teacher, a new recognition of the district leader, and a new recognition of the local leader. You must also have a new recognition of the elders and discard habitual notions about your fellow members to have a new understanding.  
If what you have remembered and known until now does not reach the standards that God desires, you must reorganize your thoughts to reach those standards 100 percent. Only then can you fully reach the standards that God desires. How much does God long for young Unification Church members who can reach those standards? If you think you have reached the standards that God desires, that is a mistaken thought. You must think again that reaching those standards is an incredibly difficult task. However, you must not be discouraged.  
Principled Prayer  
In spring, you will see the swallows that went to the south returning to build nests at the eaves of your house. After a while, they will lay eggs, and in about 40 days, you will see the chicks flying. While they grow in that nest, they must endure the hardships of a narrow space, but once they mature and can fly, they can freely soar across the world. They can become magnificent swallows that can fly farther than any migratory bird and reach the south all at once.  
You are the same. The hardships and trials you endure here are to prevent you from tasting the sorrow of defeat in the practical battlefields of trials that will come in the future. You must go through multiple trials here and arm yourselves with new beliefs. When you become like swallows that can fly toward a new heaven, you will surely understand how blessed this foundation is. Therefore, what you eat here is more precious than anything else in your life, and what you wear and sleep in here is more valuable than anything else.  
In the new era, you must believe in new truths. Members in the regions must always pray principled prayers.  
You must not say, "God, I pray here in any region, anywhere tonight." When you pray to God, you must reveal your affiliation. If you are from the southern part of the headquarters church, you must say you are from the southern part and have the direction toward the headquarters church, identifying yourself as someone from any region of any district. Why must you do this? It is to respect the historical tradition.  
Then, you must pray for the members you are currently overseeing, that is, those who are horizontally connected to you. I have a responsibility to bring light to them and to serve them. I lack the strength to fulfill this responsibility, so please give me strength. Such prayers are effective.  
The more important the prayer, the more it should be done with the same heart as those who are devoted at the headquarters church. This is how the method of prayer should be. You must become friends with a tearful heart, tracing the historical connections and backgrounds that the headquarters church has walked through until now. God is with you there. If there is someone praying at the headquarters church centered on God's will, they should have the heart to pray from a position of greater loyalty.  
You must pray, saying that you will do the work done at the headquarters church here as well. Yet, despite this, you do not pray that way. When you observe the prayers, the movements may also reflect that.  
Our Responsibility in the Mainstream  
Members of the Unification Church must strive for their assigned posts. If something good happens while you are responsible for a certain region, you should say, "Father, thank you." When something good happens, do not just rejoice in that place. Instead, pray, "God, please be pleased with this work that has arisen from the headquarters." After praying like this, report to your district leader or regional leader, and then you can rejoice.  
A person who lives with such a mindset will not encounter obstacles on their path. If the fate of unification is a progressive historical fate, as long as that fate remains, there will be absolutely no obstacles on the path that person takes. What was once blocked will instead bring benefits as a result of good, rather than binding that person with evil.  
Where do you intend to belong? You must belong to God's side. However, even among God's side, there are mainstream and branch lines, and you must take pride in belonging to the mainstream of the Unification Church.  
Those belonging to the mainstream must be like a tree that sprouts leaves in spring. In summer, the leaves should become lush and flowers should bloom, and in autumn, there should be fruit. The tree must receive nutrients in a timely manner to grow together. When the leaves grow, the branches grow, the trunk grows, and the roots grow. They grow from the same standpoint. That is the essence of the tree. In other words, as the Unification Church develops, you must also develop.  
Whether developing through a national foundation or a local foundation, the scope may be small, but the form must be the same. Problems arise in places that cannot do this, and you must realize that you are in a deficient position.  
To realize this, the four directions must be determined. That is, whether it is the northern or southern hemisphere, whether it is north or south of the equator must be determined. The position is specified after the relationships of up and down, front and back, and left and right are established. Your heavenly position must also be the same. You must establish your value and determine your position based on the degrees of the four directions. Only then can you align with the current situation and maintain the correct posture; otherwise, you will end up in a negative posture. If that happens, you will inevitably be swept away by the flow of history. The Unification Church must understand that it cannot develop by following the trajectory of the world's progress.  
As you come and go this time, you must clearly remember how to serve God. You must clearly remember God, clearly remember the path of restoration, clearly remember the Teacher, clearly remember the district and regional leaders, and clearly remember that you must possess the spirit of the Unification Church to develop. You must clearly remember what kind of posture you should take in the relationship of up and down.  
Principle of Multiplication  
There must be a top for there to be a bottom, and there must be a front for there to be a back. There cannot be a lower and upper relationship. When you observe yourselves, you tend to think from your own perspective downwards, which is a lower perspective. When you think from yourself, it becomes lower. However, since the upper comes first, you must respect the upper first. If you love the upper more than the two who come together in harmony, you will develop faster.  
That is why the Bible says that if two people agree on earth and pray, anything will be accomplished. Between God and humans, God is the upper and humans are the lower.  
In a vertical relationship of upper and lower, multiplication does not occur. To multiply, a division action must take place. And it must be on a horizontal line. When it is on a horizontal line, multiplication occurs automatically.  
In a vertical relationship like that of a regional leader and a district leader, multiplication does not occur. However, when they unite and the regional leader acts with the district leader, multiplication occurs. This is the principle of creation.  
Why do we do evangelism? It is for multiplication. Multiplication does not occur in a vertical relationship. It must be on a horizontal level, united and exchanging with each other. Therefore, you must unite with the members centered around the church leader on a horizontal level. Only then will there be development in every aspect.
Focusing on the regional leaders, the call for unity among church leaders is to develop everything through that unity, and the same goes for the call for regional leaders to unite around the district leader to further advance. Development, in other words, means multiplication. When you pledge your loyalty, there is a multiplication that occurs there, dozens of times over. 

Time does not fluctuate. It is the human heart that fluctuates, so even if individuals are active in various regions, they must stand on a horizontal standard centered on the news from the headquarters. Just as all sensations felt within the body reach the cells simultaneously through the nervous system, all members should be in a position to resonate simultaneously with the news from the headquarters. Only then can they possess a normal life. Therefore, it is natural for you to miss the headquarters.

However, if you only relate through a vertical standard, as is conveyed through the nervous system, you may feel it temporarily, but you will not continue to feel it. When we look at the bone structure of our body, it is orderly connected both vertically and horizontally.

Let’s remember, let’s remember once again. What is it that you should carry in your heart as you come and go from the headquarters? It is to remember, to remember once again. You must clearly understand that your character is determined by how much you transcend habitual emotions.

Therefore, in dealing with the headquarters church, with the district, with the region, and with each individual, you must innovate the position you have taken until now. There will be no development until you recognize from a new perspective. New creativity cannot arise. That is how the principle of creation works.

The four-stage doubling movement is one of the four major goals we have set for this year. It is not a problem to have a grand ideal to exceed this. However, if you adopt an attitude of avoiding sacrifice, and if last year was difficult, this year will be even more impossible. Therefore, you must remember this tremendous goal for this year. You must realize God’s heart, God’s circumstances, and God’s wishes.

By doing so, you must create an internal expectation of heart and fulfill the four-stage doubling movement or activities aimed at economic recovery to achieve all of this. When looking at these issues, you cannot rely on the conceptual understanding you have heard through the district leader until now. The recognition that is thoroughly remembered must become the source of actions that can move and explode your entire body. If the amount of explosive power is less than last year, you will become a dropout in the seven-year course.

Therefore, you must remember once again. You must remember the district leader you have known until now and the regional leader once again. You must remember once again in the place where you are weary. The reason your heart is weary is not because of God but because the cause lies within yourself. God does not block the path of those who are victorious. God leads those who have devoted themselves to the path of victory. Therefore, if you have devoted yourself, there will be no despair or weariness that causes you to fall.

The reason you are weary on the path of your mission is that you are thinking centered on yourself rather than centered on God. Starting from oneself and ending in ruin is a testament to being a fallen descendant. If starting from oneself becomes the same as starting from God, then restoration will happen automatically, right?

You have heard this tremendous word about atoning for the history of sins accumulated until now, but have you stood at the forefront of atonement and restoration, holding onto God and struggling? Have you truly stood at the forefront of atonement and restoration centered on the district leader responsible for the blueprint, the regional leader responsible for the county, and the church leader responsible for the town, and confronted Satan?

When facing difficulties, you must recall what you should remember. You must look back at the history you have lived through until now, observe the present, and move toward the future. You must run so that the newly remembered and recognized can capture your heart. You must clearly understand that without this resolution and belief, you cannot achieve your intended purpose.

So what should you remember? To achieve your intended purpose, there must be difficulties. It is natural that there should be difficulties.

Every time you encounter such difficulties, you must recall the image of Grandpa Noah, who, for 120 years, faced the criticism and ridicule of those around him while holding onto the ark and carving wood to build it. You must not forget the hard work of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, who, over three generations, struggled to restore the heavenly connection and achieve the original purpose that God sought. How difficult was the 120 years that Noah walked for the people of Israel?

The reason the people of Israel have not stood before God’s will until now and have become a nation that has been abused by many nations and rejected globally is because they committed the foolishness of not receiving Jesus. However, Jesus prayed with blood in the Garden of Gethsemane and, while carrying the cross, ascended Golgotha without caring for His own destruction. He was solely determined and resolved with God. You must recall this unwavering internal resolution.

At some point, have you ever prayed while crying out, “My Father!” like Jesus did in the Garden of Gethsemane? Have you stood in the position of Jesus, who, despite criticism, ridicule, mockery, and whipping, resolutely carried the cross toward Golgotha, prepared for death? Have you also recalled all the past connections of our ancestors? The historical stories must be re-enacted today and atoned for by you as a principle of restoration. Therefore, you should think that you have been placed in such conditions in this era. 

Thus, like Noah, Abraham, and Moses, you must strive to understand God’s sorrow and sadness and the hearts of historical ancestors. When you shed tears, they must not be worthless tears. Do not become cheap by being swayed by the words of a stranger, nor become someone who forsakes their path of life for the words of one person. Even if a storm arises, you must pledge to stand firm and become a weapon that can defeat that enemy. You must become those who make such a pledge, rather than those who collapse amidst the incoming storm and chaotic environment.

When you think from the perspective of God and your ancestors, how much have you experienced the heart of Jesus praying with blood in the Garden of Gethsemane and heading toward Golgotha in the historical course? How much of the path that Noah endured for 120 years have you walked? How much have you walked the path of Moses, who cast aside his glory and was consumed with patriotism for his homeland, Israel, moving toward God’s will without caring for death? You must step forward and become individuals who can comfort them as you trace back through history. When you clearly understand that you are the ones who must comfort all ancestors in such a position, you cannot be weary.

Even when you see your ancestors in this way, you cannot be weary. Only then can you establish even a single condition to restore the mistakes made by your ancestors in the past. You cannot rely solely on what your ancestors have done. Yet, despite this, you are thinking centered on yourself rather than centered on God. No matter how miserable and painful your situation may be, can you compare it to the sorrowful heart of God who lost His sons and daughters and has walked for 6,000 years to find them?

God, while facing sorrow, curses, and terrible environments in the course of history, has never thought of us as unfilial children for even a single day. Rather, He has been working to save us. When you think of the God who dreams of a new hopeful heaven and has been working on the providence of salvation, you must think from that standpoint of God and participate in what He is doing. By doing so, you become a historical ancestor. If you think about this and truly feel it, there is no reason to despair or become weary. If you do not clearly recognize this after hearing such words, pray, pray. Pray centered on the principle of restoration.

When God created Adam and Eve, how much sincerity did He put into their creation? Adam and Eve fell without knowing this. How sorrowful must God have been when Adam and Eve fell? When Adam and Eve fell, God tried to restore through Cain and Abel. But when that was broken, how sorrowful must God have felt? If you had stood in such a position, what would have happened? You must not be like that.

You must pray from the standpoint of Noah. If it is Abraham, you must pray from Abraham’s standpoint; if it is Moses, you must pray from Moses’ standpoint. If it is John the Baptist, you must pray from John the Baptist’s standpoint. You must pray from the position of the unfortunate John the Baptist, who failed to recognize Jesus despite having to recognize Him. You must also pray from the standpoint of Jesus, who struggled during His three years of public ministry. You must pray from the position of Jesus, who bore the responsibility of gathering the entire nation that betrayed Him and setting up the altar of God, giving the results of victory back to God, and from the position of Jesus, who bore the responsibility of restoring not only the people of Israel but also countless fallen humanity around the world. You must also pray from the standpoint of the teacher you have known until now.

What should you think about and what should you pray for? It is not enough to think and pray only for your small town, county, or province. While there may be many complicated stories surrounding the current situation in Korea, that is not the issue. There are even more tremendous global issues at stake, and you must be in a position to worry and pray about those. Therefore, the suffering occurring domestically cannot even be considered a suffering. But can you become weary? Especially the passionate young men and women in their twenties.

So there are many young people in the Unification Church. If you are asked to take up arms in such an environment, you must not become a group that slanders. In the final hand-to-hand combat, you must be the one who takes the weapons and fights fiercely, rather than becoming someone who struggles to love only their own individuality in such a position.

When you are welcomed in place of the ancestors who were mistreated and not welcomed in this land, you must be grateful. If they appear even in dreams, you should be able to say, “I will not receive it, so please receive it.” You should be happy with that internal emotional standard; otherwise, you will be unknowingly dragged along.

Therefore, when you go out to such a place, you must cut your hair short. You must go out with your belt tightened. At that time, you will have many possibilities to see what appears before your eyes and smile. You must approach it from a perspective that can digest it and pray to God each time. You must return the ideals that Abraham could not face and the burdens that Noah could not resolve, through God, to the ancestors of countless generations.

You must have the attitude that you are unworthy of being welcomed because you are a servant of servants. Then you will not fall or be dragged along by Satan from an emotional standard. If you cannot do this, you will most likely be dragged along.

Especially at this time when we emphasize economic restoration, it is even more so. When you think of all the backgrounds you have lived through, if you become weary, what good will it do? Regional leaders used to find it as difficult as reaching for the stars to seek 1,000 won, but now they think nothing of 10,000 won or even 100,000 won. The reason the teacher has emphasized economic restoration through enterprises until now is to make it a foundation for your life, a stepping stone for God, and to help uplift your heart. However, it is truly regrettable to think that it has instead become a material that sells your heart.

When thinking about various issues, you must clearly understand that you cannot help but emphasize the creation of internal emotional expectations once again.

You, who have stepped forward on behalf of God and the nation, are not doing the anti-communist lectures for just a few people. Communism, on the path of restoration, is inevitably the satanic force that must be crushed. God is striving to establish a victorious nation, so you must have the heart that you cannot be welcomed until the day the entire nation welcomes you. When the nation welcomes you, you must approach it with a humble heart, wanting to place all the righteous who have come and gone before God to make Him happy.

Now, you must not stand in the place of being welcomed. That is a process. You still have many hills to cross and many paths to run. You must remember that if there are obstacles in the way of that path, you must become those who are determined to overcome them. If you do not do this, you will sell out the tradition you have built up until now. The greatest achievement established in the struggle of the seven-year course is precisely that tradition. But to sell this out would be disastrous.

The teacher has worked while wearing a jacket until now. He has worn ragged clothes without shame and has boasted about it. However, for the ambassador, he must have the necessary environmental conditions and establish external prestige, so now he wears a suit. This is to face God and to establish God’s prestige. But when he returns home, he puts on the old appearance again. You must not feel sad or dislike the teacher for adopting such a look. Such things should not happen. Those who dislike this are Satan.

The development of a factory is due to the abilities of the factory manager. When that person goes out into the city, they change into clean clothes. When they return to the factory, they must change their clothes again. However, if they do not want to take off the new clothes they wore when they went out and do not want to change into work clothes when they come back, they cannot become the factory manager. In other words, if they do not want to put on those oil-stained clothes again and do not want to touch the machines, they will lose the foundation they have cleaned up. You may easily find yourself in that same position. Yet, when you find yourself in a miserable environment, shedding tears and feeling miserable, you must know that God is walking the same path as you.
S先生은 공장에 갈 때 될 수 있으면 양복을 입고 가지 않습니다. S선생님이 마음으로 결심한 책임이 있기 때문에 같이 일하지 못하는 것이 한입니다. 여러분을 길러 줄 보금자리는 어디냐? 환영받는 자리가 보금자리가 아닙니다. 천국이나 궁전처럼 만민이 우러러보는 자리나 쉴 수 있는 안식의 터전이 보금자리가 아닙니다. 그런 자리를 버리고 십자가를 지고 싸워 승리한 자리에서 하나님의 위로를 받을 수 있는 곳이 보금자리라는 것입니다. 하나님이 해주시는 위로를 크게 여겨야지, 세상에서 보내 주는 위로를 좋아하면 나라를 팔아먹게 된다는 것을 여러분은 다시 한번 생각해야 합니다.

경제복귀를 위해서 정성을 다하라 금년에는 경제적 기반 확립을 위해서 움직여야 합니다. 여러분이 사업을 나가니 기성교인들이 통일교회 젊은이들은 장사한다, 비종교 단체다라고 하는데, 그것에 개의치 말아야 합니다. 우리가 경제복귀 하는 데 있어서 호화찬란한 자리에서 하는 것을 선생님은 원치 않습니다. 환영받는 자리에서 하는 것은 더더욱 원치 않습니다. 오지 말라고 해도 가야 합니다. 민족이 전부 환영했더라면 지금까지 복귀섭리를 해오지 않았을 것입니다. 나는 삼천만 민족이 서로 위할 수 있는 그런 통일의 민족을 만들어 봤으면 좋겠다는 것입니다. 여러분이 좋은 자리에서 그것을 거두었다면 그것은 적은 탕감이 됩니다. 어려운 자리에서도 그것을 규합하여 거둔다면 더 귀하다는 것입니다. 선생님은 그렇게 생각합니다.

여러분이 고통스러울지라도 그 하나의 물건을 팔기 위하여 들이는 정성은 어떤 상인보다 더 진지해야 합니다. 다른 장사꾼보다 몇 배의 심정적인 기준을 갖게 되면 더 비싼 물건도 머리 숙이고 사게 되는 것입니다. 그런 소비자의 수가 금년에 얼마나 더 되겠습니까? 그렇게 하려면 보통 정성 가지고는 안 돼요. 그러므로 여러분들은 자기의 책임진 분야로 돌아가서 만사에 대해 기도드리며 정성을 다해야 합니다. 그래야 뜻을 이루는 거예요. 지역장들이 모인 데서 지구장이 큰소리치면 기분 나빠합니다. 기분 나빠할 수 있는 간판을 하나님으로부터 받았어요? 그러나 기분 나빠할 수 있는 그런 자리가 망하는 자리가 아니요, 잘만 이겨낸다면 여러분이 승리할 수 있는 기반을 닦는 것입니다. 그러므로 여러분들은 돌아가게 되면 그냥 그 대로 나갈 것이 아니라 이러한 전후좌우를 알고 하나님을 중심삼아서 지금까지의 자기 자세를 반성하고, 다시 한번 새로운 입장에서 움직여 주기를 바랍니다. 알겠지요?「예.」

하늘의 사람이 되려면 여러분, 시의시대가 무엇입니까?「모심의 생활을 하는 시대입니다.」여러분, 지금은 시위시대예요, 시의시대예요? 그런데 요즘 시위하는 사람들이 많습니다. 그렇다고 해서 시의인지 시위인지 괜히 알쏭달쏭해 하지 마세요. 여러분은 시의시대, 즉 모심의 생활에 있어서 정확한 중심을 두고 나가야 됩니다. 하나님을 모시는 데에는 법도가 있습니다. 그 법도를 어길 때에는 하나님은 무척 노여워하시는 분입니다. 자식을 사랑하는 부모가 자식의 말 한마디에 따라 가슴에 못이 박혔다, 빠졌다 하는 것과 같이 하나님께서도 인간을 사랑하시기 때문에 노여움이 많으신 분입니다. 그렇기 때문에 자칫 잘못하면 하나님으로부터 노여움을 사게 됩니다. 그렇기 때문에 언제나 선생님도 선생님대로 하나님을 기쁘게 해드리려고 합니다. 옷을 입을 때도 잘 입어야 합니다. 선생님도 옷을 잘 입은 사람을 보면 기분이 참 좋습니다. 그래서 선생님도 그래야 되겠다는 생각을 하고 양복을 입고 나왔습니다. 그렇지 않으면 잠바를 입고 나왔을 것입니다.

면에서 칭찬받기 위해 생활하는 사람은 잘할 때는 칭찬을 받겠지만 거기에서 한번 실수하는 날에는 아주 완전히 망하는 것입니다. 그렇지만 그 사람이 면에서 칭찬받고서 군에서도 칭찬받겠다고 열심히 충성하면 살길이 남게 됩니다. 그러나 군에서도 칭찬을 받겠다고 눈이 벌개져서 돌아다니다가 한 번 실수하면 그 사람은 오히려 망하게 되는 것입니다. 그렇지만 군을 잊어버리고 도를 위한 목표를 정하고 나가게 될 때는 군에서 실수하더라도 또 살아남을 수 있게 되는 것입니다. 그러니 우리 통일교인들은 하나님을 제일 사랑해서 하나님의 칭찬을 받아야 하는 것입니다. 세계의 어떠한 대통령이 해주는 칭찬이 문제가 아닙니다. 하나님으로부터 칭찬을 받은 체험만이 영원히 남아지는 것입니다. 그런데 아직까지 하나님으로부터 칭찬을 받을 수 있는 때가 못 되었습니다.

선생님은 우리 통일교회가 대한민국에서만 칭찬받기를 원하는 것이 아닙니다. 또한 세계의 30억 인류가 칭찬한다 해도 그것에 만족하지 않을 것입니다. 수많은 영인들이 환영할 수 있고 하나님께서 고맙다고 칭찬할 수 있는 그 자리까지 나아가야 된다는 것입니다. 그것은 엄청나게 먼 기준입니다.

내가 3년 동안 수고하고 고생했으니 반드시 칭찬받아야 되겠다는 생각을 하면 그동안 수고한 것이 모두 허사가 되는 것입니다. 민족과 세계를 위해서 3년을 수고했더라도 아직까지 수고한 자리에 들어가지 못했다고 생각하고 더 충성하겠다고 다짐해야 됩니다. 그러면 그 수고의 값이 점점 더 세계적으로 뻗어나가게 되어 맨 끝에는 크나큰 칭찬, 즉 세계적인 칭찬을 받을 수 있는 자리에 세워지게 되는 것입니다. 그래야 하늘의 사람이 되는 것입니다.

선생님이 걸어온 길 선생님이 여러분들을 지역장을 시키고, 또 여러분들에게 한국을 책임지라고 한 말이 무슨 말인지 알겠습니까? 전부 다 아프리카, 남미, 구라파 등 세계의 오대양 육대주로 내보내기 위해서였습니다. 그런데 한국에는 그런 생각을 갖고 있는 사람이 없다는 것입니다. 일본 사람을 봐도 전부 다 일본을 떠나서 세계 복귀를 위해 힘쓰고 있는데, 한국의 통일교회 청년들 중에는 그런 사람이 없다는 것입니다. 있어요, 없어요?「있습니다.」있긴 뭐가 있어? 그러려면 여건을 갖추어야 됩니다.

여러분이 수고하고, 고생해 놓고 칭찬받겠다는 입장에 서면 그 여건을 갖출 수 없습니다. 그렇기 때문에 자기에게 맡겨진 책임을 중심삼고 면을 통해서 군을, 군을 통해서 도를 움직이겠다고 생각해야 됩니다. 또 도를 통해서 이 나라를 움직이겠다고 생각하라는 것입니다. 선생님은 이렇게 걸어왔습니다.

선생님은 조그만 토담집에서 어렵게 살면서도 오늘은 무슨 반찬을 먹었으니 내일은 또 어떤 것을 먹어야 할까 하는 그런 걱정 속에서 살지 않았습니다. 비록 옷은 남루하고 밥은 굶는 처지에 있었지만 생각만큼은 이 세상을 정복하고 하늘나라를 꼭 이루겠다고 했고, 그럴 수 있다고 큰소리를 꽝꽝 쳤습니다.

그러므로 여러분도 지방에 가서 단칸방 또는 동네 사람들이 들어가지 않는 방, 즉 나이가 많아 죽게 된 사람이 들어가 살다가 숨진 그런 땅에서 생활을 하게 되더라도 천하를 통일할 수 있는 터를 남겨야 합니다. 그리고 그 터 위에 교회를 세운다면 하늘이 얼마나 귀하게 여기겠습니까?

그렇기 때문에 그 부락 하나만을 중심삼고 다닌다고 생각하지 말라는 것입니다. 그리고 거기에서 칭찬받은 것을 전체로 생각해서는 안 됩니다. 그런 것은 흔히 있을 수 있는 일입니다. 지나가는 길손에게 점심 한 끼니를 대접하면 그 길손이 고맙다는 말을 하는 것과 같은 것으로 생각하라는 것입니다.

그런 생각을 가지고, 기분 나쁜 일이 생겼다고 해서 아이쿠 나 억울해서 못살겠네. 하면서 자기 가슴에 맺힌 감정을 하나님 앞에 호소하는 그런 기도는 하지 말라는 것입니다. 이것을 잘 극복하고 뜻을 위해 죽겠다는 자리까지 나아가야 합니다. 무슨 일에든지 그럴 수 있다는 생각을 해야지만 뜻 앞에 조건이 세워지는 것입니다. 이 조건에 걸리는 사람은 욕심이 많은 사람입니다. 욕심이 많은 사람은 눈앞에 있는 것은 다 자기 것이라고 생각하기 때문에 조건에 걸린다는 것입니다.

교회에 누군 뭐 어떻고, 누군 뭐 어떻다고 하는 사람들은 전부 다 욕심이 많습니다. 아무리 없을망정 절대 그래서는 안 됩니다. 무엇이 없고, 무엇이 없고 하는 것도 다 시련 무대에서 하나님이 나를 교훈하기 위해서 나오는 것이요, 나를 교육시키기 위한 교재로 등장하는 것이라고 생각해야 되는 것입니다. 선생님은 그렇게 생각하고 있습니다. 그러므로 모든 것을 참회하여 그 환경에서 여러분들은 책임을 다해야 됩니다. 알겠지요?「예.」

모심과 축복 여러분 시의가 무엇입니까? 모시는 거지요? 그러면 여러분은 얼마만큼 모셔 봤습니까?

여러분들은 어디에서든지 배고플 때나 혹은 몹시 어려울 때에 도움을 받게 되면 큰 고마움을 느낄 것입니다. 선생님도 그런 때가 있었습니다. 지금도 학창시절, 어려웠을 때 도와준 사람을 잊지 않고 있습니다. 그래서 이 7년 동안 선생님이 조건만 세우면 그때는 전부 다 갚으려고 생각하고 있습니다. 선생님은 지금까지 복귀의 길을 걸어오면서 서러움을 당하는 환경에 있을 때 선생님에게 은혜를 베푼 사람들을 다 기억하고 있습니다. 즉 선생님이 신세진 것을 다 갚으려고 생각하고 있습니다. 그런데 지금까지 왜 안 갚았느냐? 그것은 지금 갚으면 작은 갚음밖에 안 되기 때문입니다. 선생님이 한 가지 섭섭하게 생각하고 있는 것이 있습니다. 선생님이 이북에서 피난을 내려올 때에 선생님에게 도움을 준 평안도 친구가 있었습니 다. 그 사람에 대해 뼈에 사무치게 고마워하고 있고, 지금도 그 고마움을 잊지 못하고 있습니다. 그래서 선생님은 이 7년노정이 끝나고 신세를 갚을 수 있는 때가 오면 우리 통일교회 교인들 집은 못 지어 주더라도 그에게 집을 지어 주려고 생각하고 있었습니다. 그런 사람들을 앞으로 융숭히 대접하여 본때를 보여야 되겠다고 생각했습니다. 선생님이 이렇게 다 마음에 생각하고 있었는데 그 사람이 어느 한때 식구들에게 와 가지고, 당신네 선생이 어려울 때에 내가 협조를 했으니 여러분들이 나를 도와주시오. 하는 것을 선생님이 보았을 때 무척 안타까웠습니다. 그래서 박복한 사람이로구만. 조금만 더 참지. 하고 생각했습니다. 선생님은 그렇게 배은망덕한 사람이 아닙니다. 선생님은 그렇게 하려는 깊은 뜻이 있었다는 것입니다. 무슨 말인지 알겠어요?「예.」

여러분은 하나님을 모신 자로서 여러분이 기쁠 때 하나님을 얼마나 기쁘게 해 드렸습니까? 여러분들이 배고플 때 밥을 먹으면서 느끼는 고마움 이상으로 하나님을 모셔 드려야 되는 것입니다.

여러분들은 좋은 것을 먹을 때나 입을 때, 그리고 슬플 때나 어려울 때에도 항상 하나님을 모셔야 합니다. 그래서 하나님의 마음에 기억될 수 있는 사연들을 남겨 놓아야 합니다.

여러분이 통일교회에서 출세하려면 지방 교회 교회장의 마음을 점령하여 그 교회장의 마음에 남아지는 사람이 되어야 합니다. 즉 동네면 동네 가운데서 먼저 남아질 수 있는 사람, 교회장의 축복을 옮겨 받을 수 있는 사람이 되어야 하는 것입니다. 그 다음에는 지역장의 마음에 남아지고, 지구장의 마음에 남아지고, 더 나아가서는 협회장의 마음에 남아져야 합니다. 그래야 선생님의 마음에 남아지는 것입니다. 이렇게 단계를 거쳐야 되는 것입니다.

7년노정은 모심의 생활에 대한 준비 과정 그렇기 때문에 여러분들이 윗사람들의 마음에 남아지려면 정성들여야 합니다. 그러기 위해서는 좋은 것 하나라도 있으면 더 주고 싶은 마음이 여러분에게 충만해야 됩니다.

심정의 세계에서는 물건을 갖고 통하는 것이 아닙니다. 마음으로 통하는 것입니다. 항상 감사하는 마음으로 윗사람이 슬플 때 같이 슬퍼할 수 있고, 기쁠 때 같이 기뻐할 수 있는 인연을 가지고 통하는 것입니다. 그렇게 사는 사람에게 하나님은 함께하시는 것입니다. 그래서 그가 슬퍼할 때 하나님도 슬퍼하시고, 그가 기뻐할 때 하나님도 기뻐하시는 것입니다.

그렇기 때문에 여러분들이 이러한 단계를 거치지 않고 지구장을 대하고, 지역장을 대해서는 안 되는 것입니다.

모시는 데 있어서는 단계가 있는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 통일교회 교인이 되었다 할진대는 누구든지 7년노정을 다 거쳐야 합니다. 즉 7년노정은 모심의 생활에 대한 준비의 과정으로서 타락한 인간들에게 절대적인 과정으로 남아져 있는 것입니다.

그런데도 불구하고 7년노정에 대해서 많은 사람들이 모르고 있습니다. 다 잊어버렸습니다. 여러분은 어떻습니까? 7년노정이 뭐야? 다 그저 그렇지. 이렇게 생각해서는 안 됩니다. 그렇기 때문에 가정으로 말하면 두 사람이 살면 네 사람이 사는 생활을 해야 됩니다. 즉 부모를 모셔야 되는 것입니다. 그러나 부모만 모셔 가지고는 안 됩니다. 더 나아가서 그 아들까지 모셔야 된다는 것입니다. 알겠어요?

그렇기 때문에 여러분 자신이 사위기대를 복귀하기 위해서는 부모만 모셔서는 안 됩니다. 반드시 그 아들까지 모셔야 되는 것입니다. 이렇게 해서 여러분의 모든 정성을 그 앞에 연결시켜야 됩니다. 그렇게 되면 외적인 면에서는 두 사람이 살지만 내적인 면에서는 자그마치 네 사람, 다섯 사람의 생활 터전이 되는 것입니다.

부모를 모시는 데는 3년을 모셔야 됩니다. 왜 3년이냐? 3수 과정을 한꺼번에 복귀하기 위해서입니다. 그러므로 여러분들이 가정을 중심삼고 살게 될 때에는, 선생님이 언제 어느 때고 예고 없이 여러분이 사는 집을 방문하더라도 선생님이 잘 수 있는 방이 있어야 됩니다. 방이 없으면 자리라도 있어야 합니다. 그 자리는 정성들인 곳이라야 합니다.

그렇기 때문에 그 자리를 중심삼고 단간방(단칸방이라는 뜻의 북한어)이라도 언제나 정성들인 한 곳을 만들어 놓아야 된다는 것입니다. 그리하여 부모를 모실 수 있는 한 날이 오면 옷을 입어도 준비된 옷을 입고, 신발을 신어도 준비된 신발을 신고 깨끗하게 해 가지고 모실 준비를 해야 합니다. 빗자루를 들고 마당을 쓸더라도 한 번 더 쓸어야 되겠습니다. 그리고 부모를 천번 만번 회상해야 되겠습니다. 여러분들, 그렇게 해 봤습니까? 그렇게 해 봤어요? 살아 있는 교회가 되려면 다 그래야 되는 것입니다. 교회에는 아버님이 와서 기도할 수 있는 곳이 있어야 된다는 것입니다. 평소에 심정의 촛불을 켜 놓고 정성을 들여야 됩니다.

그리워하는 마음을 가져라 요즈음 지역장들을 보게 되면 껄렁껄렁한 지역장들이 많습니다. 총 팔러 다니다 보니 예배드리는 날이 됐는데도 예배는 식구들끼리 보고 있고 자기 는 그날도 모르는 지역장들이 많습니다. 제사는 누가 관리하느냐? 제사장이 관리하는 것입니다. 그렇지요? 제사는 객이 관리해서는 안 되는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 여러분들이 지방에서도 공적인 회합 자리를 중요시하지 않는다면 발전을 못 합니다. 알겠어요, 지역장들? 구역예배도 마찬가지입니다.

주일날 예배 때에는 반드시 목욕재계하고 하나님 앞에 경배를 드리고, 또한 성지에 찾아가서 기도해야 합니다. 비록 찾아드는 사람이 없을망정 하나님이 그 부락을 굽어살피고 거기에 동역할 수 있는 심정적인 터전을 닦아 놓아야 합니다. 하나님 앞에 혼자 기도하며 눈물 흘리는 그 자리는 절대 외롭지 않습니다. 하나님이 같이하시니 절대로 외롭지가 않다는 것입니다. 3년 이상 여러분들이 정성을 들였는데도 그 동네에서 찾는 자가 없다면 그 동네는 망하는 것입니다.

여러분이 손톱을 깎는 그 시간에도 아버님을 모실 수 있는 그때 그 시간을 오면 어떻게 할 것이냐? 어떻게 효도를 할 것이냐? 그리고 어떤 모습으로 아버님을 모실 것인가를 생각해야 합니다. 아버님을 어느 강가에서 만날 수 있을 것인가! 어떤 곳에서 만날 수 있을 것인가!

여러분들이 두메산골에 들어가서 생활하게 되면 우리 통일교회 식구들이 찾아와 주었으면 하고 간절히 바라게 되고, 또 식구 중에 누가 아픈 것이 아닌가 하고 염려하게 됩니다. 그리고 자기와 제일 가까운 식구를 맞이했으면 좋겠다. 또 선생님을 맞이했으면, 지구장을 맞이했으면, 지역장을 맞이했으면 좋겠다 하는 그리움이 있어야 합니다.
