Unification begins with relationships. So how are relationships formed? They arise from areas of interest.

How many people know that they have entered the Unification Church at a precious time? The ideology is good, but it is difficult to act. One should not say, "I don't like the Teacher's method." To win, we must not be divided. The restoration providence aims for complete unification and complete victory. The Teacher should not work alone. By matching your steps together, each person's position is determined. Otherwise, there will be much regret after the restoration history is over.

The victory of the Unification Church is determined by how much interest and effort one puts into the purpose, and how much connection an individual has made with the Unification Church determines their position.

Jacob's 14 years of labor became the standard for family life. After 14 years, we will establish a balance in our lives.

Up to now, how much interest you have had in the church will be the key to restoration. Those who are not interested in the movement of restoration are fakes. If such people become leaders, it will break down. Therefore, how much interest you have in the church's movement will be the turning point in determining whether you become a victor or a loser.

Internal Standards for Becoming Abel
We must focus externally on external activities, while internally, those who have received grace must unite to promote the fulfillment of the purpose. In doing so, we must play the role of a beacon to save the Korean church. Until now, those who have had spiritual experiences have been completely ignored in the church. This must never happen.

Originally, the archangel was the beginning of the fall. Therefore, in restoration, the angelic world must cooperate. Only with cooperation can all be restored and liberated. Thus, the spiritual world corresponding to the angelic world must work. The fallen nature of humanity continues as long as fallen humans remain.

During Jesus' time, who had the central responsibility for the restoration through indemnity? It was with the Jewish people and the Jewish nation. At that time, the Jewish people should have fulfilled their internal mission, and the Jewish nation should have fulfilled its external mission of restoring the world.

When we encounter those who have had spiritual experiences, that is, when they come to report, we must be careful not to unconditionally obey them in our hearts. First, we should receive their words but must criticize them in light of God's providence. The principle will be the standard for that criticism.

The Teacher cannot do it alone. If done incorrectly, it can lead to serious problems. Decisions must be made in accordance with the global situation and the programs of the spiritual world. We must analyze whether they are Cain or Abel. You must determine, "You are Abel because of this and that," or "I am Abel or Cain because of this and that."

God cannot judge absolutely until He discerns this content. This is the same in worldly trials. Unification Church members easily say, "We are Abel." They can easily claim to be Abel based on their own understanding of the spiritual world.

So what is the actual internal standard for becoming Abel? It is to love God and to love God's work. And to become a sacrifice for that work. After becoming a sacrifice before Heaven, one can command Cain from the position of Abel. Therefore, if he does not listen, he must be struck. If he breaks away, all of his blessings can be inherited by you. In loving the purpose, make sure you can stand above that person! Thus, when you become a sacrifice before the purpose as Abel, Cain will inevitably have to walk the path of the purpose only through you.

The Path to Salvation
The Teacher is still carrying out heavenly work based on such standards. Those who have received spiritual experiences testify about the Teacher, and the Teacher responds to them because He sees their sincerity towards Heaven. It is fine to apply a certain formula to them and make a firm decision according to Heaven's laws.

Since 1965, the work of grace has begun again in the established church. During that time, they lost grace because they opposed the Unification Church. Now that the Unification Church has reached a 21-year period, the established church is also in a position to experience a revival.

Because when Abel's altar is established, Cain's altar must also be prepared.

In the past, there was a spirit of opposition to the Unification Church among them, but now it is time for a spirit of welcome to arise. They must come over, but in reality, it is not easy for them to do so, so we must engage in various intermediary activities to build a bridge.

Today, our members, especially the long-standing members, are losing much of the joy and grace they felt when they first entered. We must not lose the heart that rejoiced when we first entered.

The disciples who sent Jesus to the path of death received a shameful salvation. How joyful would it have been if they had died with Jesus and resurrected together? You are people who did not know this.

At first, even if someone persecuted them, those who advanced with a fervent spirit now show signs of fatigue after several years. This is evidence that their hearts have fallen away. If the joy felt when first entering the Unification Church has dulled due to some trials, the relationship with the church will become distant.

Still, I truly appreciate that you have survived without dying. However, one worrying thing is whether you can face the purpose with the heart you had when you first entered, or whether you will face it with a shameful attitude.

If we cannot rejoice more in the spiritual world than we do on earth, we will receive a shameful salvation in the afterlife. With such an attitude, we cannot save all people. Therefore, everyone must reflect.

To what extent do I love Heaven? To what extent do I love those whom the Lord loves? Have I become someone who can love even those who oppose the Lord? Only those who can answer affirmatively to these questions can save even the wicked.

First, you must be able to love the members that the Teacher loves in order to love those who oppose. If the standard of love falls, restoration cannot occur. We must not receive a shameful salvation. To receive the requirements of life and nutrients, we must always maintain a heartistic relationship.

Those who have lost the joy of the past are like those who have squandered their ancestors' wealth. We must become better today than we were yesterday, and better tomorrow than we are today in order to save this nation, the world, and ultimately even the world of Satan. For someone who loves God, loving people on earth should not be a problem. If we stand in the position for God's purpose, we can always uphold an Abel-like position.

Cain and Abel Centered on the Purpose
Today is the last day of April. We must reflect once again whether we are standing in a position of shameful salvation, that is, in the position of Cain. If we are indeed in the position of Abel, we must bear all that others avoid and all that is difficult. We must solve the most difficult problems of our parents and take on the difficulties outside as well. Therefore, we who are in the position of Abel must love our members and even love our enemies. We must love not ideologically but practically, and we must go forth with confidence in all matters to stand in a position that does not receive accusations from Satan.

This formula applies to the fulfillment of all restoration providence that forms individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. One expansion becomes the whole. Ultimately, all of humanity is one brotherhood. Therefore, when dealing with members, everyone should treat each other as older brothers and sisters.

And when we go out to fight, we must fight with the qualifications of parents. That is, even if the opponent is an enemy, in the ultimate sense, they are like our own children. Thus, our motto is: 
"With the heart of parents, using the body of a servant, let our sweat be for the land, our tears for humanity, and our blood for Heaven." Only then can we be completely restored. Creating such people is God's highest educational guideline.

We must make a new resolution in preparation for the upcoming second 7-year course. In terms of personal conduct, lifestyle, and anything else, we must never deviate from principles. From this perspective, who among the members is truly suitable?

If the Teacher were to act with human emotions, it would be insufficient to strike down those who oppose the purpose and drink their blood. However, if such people rejoice three times more than the current Unification Church members regarding the purpose, they must be forgiven. Those who could not take responsibility may not have caused the Teacher pain like the opponents, but when considering the results of history, there is little difference.

Those who opposed the purpose in the past must be forgiven if they return with three times more joy and acceptance of the purpose. Otherwise, Satan will accuse. The Teacher has also thought for several years about how to treat them in the future.

They are pitiful people. The gratitude of those who have been forgiven after committing sins is worth thousands of times more than the gratitude of those who have not sinned. If they return with a heart of gratitude thousands of times greater than ordinary people, God cannot help but forgive them.

Because God has such feelings, He can restore the whole. As long as there are parts that cannot be forgiven, those parts cannot be restored at any time. Therefore, the Unification Church must have such feelings to restore even the world of communism, which is the position of Satan. I often feel ashamed of myself for not being able to comfort God who has such feelings.

When the Teacher forgives someone, you must not say, "You must not do that." Ultimately, it is the heart that can forgive even the most wicked enemy that allows us to indemnify and transcend into the world of Satan. If the Teacher had not known this, the restoration history would not have been possible. Only through such feelings can the whole be restored.

Through these internal standards, we must also restore external, that is, social completion standards. To do this, we must fulfill our responsibilities as Abel, who can forgive not only those on Cain's side but also Satan.

How much have the authorities of the past made our lives miserable? However, now we have become close as they have come to understand us by directly witnessing the results and achievements we have built. Let us fulfill the mission of Abel! And keep the joy we felt when we first entered the church as a source of life to ignite the fire of life! Now that it is spring seasonally and providentially, we must gather again and make a fresh start. We must not receive a shameful salvation and go to the afterlife. 

In the relationship of upper and lower, are we in the position of Cain or Abel? In the relationship of before and after, who is the master? In the left and right relationship centered on the Teacher's family, who is at the center? We must clearly understand these and maintain our respective positions accordingly. In human relationships and the total relationships of the heavenly realm, we must also clearly know who is Cain and who is Abel.

In certain specific matters, an Abel can become a Cain. This relationship can be reversed depending on the time. If the Teacher had not known this, it would have already broken down.

The Path We Must Take
We must work not only for personal victory but also for global victory. Maintaining the position of Abel is not for our own sake but to achieve a global purpose. Those who walk in accordance with this global purpose will not perish even if they declare they will perish. If they perish, the providence of Heaven will be broken.

Only by following this law can we avoid the invasion of Satan. Otherwise, we will not be able to escape the incessant invasions of Satan day and night. Thus, after a few years, we will become exhausted and fall when a storm arises. Therefore, we must establish a character centered on faith and based on ideology.

I have the mission to resolve God's resentment, to resolve Jesus' resentment, and to resolve the resentment of all things on my shoulders, so when do I have the time to rest or do anything else? I hope you all strive not to receive a shameful salvation. For example, rice is necessary regardless of the type of seed. However, there are times when the type of rice becomes an issue. This means that the rice that God likes must be the type made in the Teacher's way. Otherwise, it is only used to give to beggars. Of course, everything is needed in some way.

Anyone who has fallen must return and be re-grafted onto the branches of the members.

Because the Teacher knows the purpose, He has not budged in the face of any storm, ridicule, or difficulty. Do you know the value of the purpose as much as the Teacher does? Upon closer inspection, there are many foolish young people, which is pitiful. Now that we have embarked on the path of purpose, we must not walk in shame. Even if we cannot change the steps we have taken until today, we must take new steps starting tomorrow. Therefore, the second 7-year course must be walked correctly.

The Teacher did not go to prison out of joy. He endured imprisonment to save you.

Whenever the opposition of the established power structure hindered the unfolding of Heaven's purpose, the Teacher spent 14 years from the age of 27 to fulfill familial expectations by 1960. After that, he walked for another 7 years and is now at the point where the 21-year period is about to end.

Even immediately after liberation, the Teacher tried to achieve the purpose by contacting the upper authorities, but some close pastors opposed it, causing a breakdown. If the purpose had been achieved at that time, the communist party would not have been able to flourish globally like this. Thus, ultimately, he went through three regimes afterward. This regime is Adam-type, the Chang regime is Hae-Wa type, and the Park regime is Archangel type. Now that the Park regime cooperates with the Unification Church, it signifies that we can enter into restoration in earnest. Initially, Hae-Wa lost because it was deceived by the archangel, but now we must overcome the archangel with words on God's side. In other words, we must turn it around with ideology.

The authorities recognizing our anti-communist activities with the term "victory" is similar to how Jacob became Israel by wrestling with the angel at the Jabbok River. From this perspective, I believe the signpost of victory that can fulfill the purpose has already been planted.

Now that the vertical standard of victory has been established, we need an organization to achieve horizontal victory based on this. The established church alone is not enough. We must restore the world with the ideology of unification. To do this, we must inevitably focus on philosophical, academic, and ideological foundations. 

If we look closely at this series of tasks, the anti-communist movement is being developed in relation to academia centered around ideology, the external evangelism activities are being developed centered around the church, and the principle study group movement is being developed centered around students.

We must expand our foundation using all established institutions as a stepping stone. After that, we must establish a foothold in Korea in terms of academic and ideological aspects and occupy the peaks of the world. Anti-communism, scholarship, faith, and patriotism must all be claimed to be the best by the Unification Church. From now on, we must conduct offensive and encirclement operations against Satan. Many influential figures representing various sectors are needed for this.

We did not have realistic political ambitions from the beginning, so we have no intention of becoming something like a president as others might speculate. We only aim to subdue Satan and halt his activities in order to construct a global heavenly kingdom.
only aiming to achieve their purpose. 
To this end, we must pioneer a realistic environment with adverse conditions and help the established church realize the true content of God's providence so that it can walk the appropriate path. Furthermore, we must completely overcome the ideology of material communism. *
24)
Be one who can love God
<Summary of the message> There are times when I am so amazed that I even doubt myself. Therefore, your knowledge is far too limited to measure the teacher and God. Thus, obedience is necessary for you. The final decision is made by the teacher. 
If a branch of a tree can bear fruit as it is, it can be left alone, but if not, it must be cut and grafted onto another tree. 
When the teacher leaves Korea, there is no one capable of taking over his work. Therefore, until the teacher departs, those among you who have been members for more than three years must gather about 70 people every night to regain the joy of joining. Whether I stand correctly before my purpose or not should be examined by whether I possess that joy of joining or not. 
Now, seven years have passed. The eighth year is a year of re-starting. Therefore, if we do not exceed the initial standard, we cannot improve further. Now is the time to directly oversee foreign matters as well. The teacher himself must be held accountable by God, but emotionally, he is inevitably in a position to receive sympathy. 
A person who cannot take responsibility for a nation cannot take responsibility for the world, and a person who cannot take responsibility for the world cannot take responsibility for the cosmos. When the teacher completes his world tour and returns, there must be a nationwide change of leadership. 
May 10, 1967 (Wed), former headquarters church. 
* This message was given before the teacher's departure to the United States after Wednesday worship, and it has been organized from the notes taken by former association president Yoo Hyo-won. The title was added by the editor. 
341 
The teacher left South Korea on May 28, 1946, and entered Pyongyang on June 6. This year marks the 21st year since the teacher began his public ministry. 
There is much work to be done in Japan and Europe. I intended to celebrate the anniversaries of May 28 and June 6 and then leave, but there is no time left to meet the goals set until October of this year. The work done for Korea must receive recognition from the spiritual world. Therefore, it must go through a path of trials. 
Loving this nation must become a tradition. If one does not stand in a position of loyalty and devotion regarding their responsibilities, they will become miserable. 
Those who speak ill of the teacher's life do not know his life and do not understand the circumstances of heaven. Among those around the teacher, 80 percent must be people who connect with heaven. You must rise to that standard, even if it means engaging in special fasting prayers. Otherwise, the teacher will seek out the members he desires. 
Now, everyone is in a refugee-like situation. Therefore, one should not have attachments to anything and should not try to settle down. Even upon reaching the destination, one must return to the place of repentance and shed their sins. We must live communally under a common purpose. How can we reach the destination with many belongings during a flight? That is the problem. 
Who will God look upon to help the Unification Church? You must become someone who can ask me for help. You must live in such a way that God can say He cooperates because of you. You must be someone through whom God can help, centered on me. This is the teacher's philosophy of life and a secret. 
You must become someone whom God cannot help but love the Republic of Korea because of you. You must become a responsible figure. However, the question is whether God can support the Unification Church by looking at you. 
You must not hate even your enemies. You must not rejoice in seeing your enemies perish. If God rejoiced at the downfall of enemies, this world could not remain. Since God cannot even hate Satan, neither can the teacher. You too must become someone who can say that God loves the Unification Church because of you. 
Chairman Yoo is an intellectual, yet his greatness lies in his unconditional faith and action. 
342   Be one whom God can love
You must push forward with a single-minded and sincere heart. There can be no shame in loving God more than anyone else. The secret to exceeding human responsibility by more than 5 percent is simply obedience. When evaluating a person, one must analyze and assess them from a standpoint of loyalty and devotion that surpasses theirs; otherwise, one will be judged themselves. You must establish a bond of father and son between God and yourself. The question is how much you have felt the heart of a parent. The teacher will guide you on such life issues. 
For fallen humanity to be perfected, they must establish a principled condition of indemnity. This is because they must go through the principle of indemnity. Only after knowing the principle and fighting to victory can one achieve perfection. 
How much does God love the area each person is responsible for? You must know that. The question is whether the factory I work in can be loved through me. There are times when the factory established by the teacher does not work well due to the mistakes of the members, but there are also times when help comes from elsewhere. 
The teacher did not speak even when he was beaten or tortured in prison. In such situations, no matter how much one prays, it is of no use. This is because the mental attitude is the issue. The teacher loves the world more than himself, which is why God loves the world through the teacher. Every time I was in prison, I tried to establish that standard of loyalty and also governed myself accordingly. 
God loves Korea. Why would He love it? I teach my mother how God can love this country through this family. 
The seven-year period after 1960 is a time for the teacher to establish a familial standard. Therefore, my mother worried whether there was anything she had not set as an example for the members. And this period is a time for the members to complete their individuality. The next seven-year period will be a time to establish families and find family members. 
During the first world tour, the teacher traveled with dirt and stones, but this time he intends to leave with a heart. *
25)
Prayer and practice
<Summary of the message> In the spring garden of love, we can resurrect in a wide and deep love that melts all cells. We cannot enter heaven without establishing three standards of love on earth. 
Jesus introduced love but did not feel its reality. When one enters the Unification Church, initially, there is a heart like that of a son or daughter, and later, feelings arise like those of a bride and groom, or parents. 
Now is the time for the feelings of rebirth, growth, and perfection to come all at once. To achieve a complete personality, one must absorb God's character. That is, one must be able to receive and absorb the character of all people. Only then can one govern all things. We must be able to align the hearts of at least twelve people. This is because all humans are manifestations of God's character. 
The teacher has no enemies. If you give everything, you can gain everything. A person who dislikes others cannot become a leader. 
You must live in a house without walls. In communal living (more than 120 people), you must become someone who can absorb their character. Jesus could not stand on such a standard while on earth. 
The way to restore grace is to practice what has been prayed for more than ten times. 
May 11, 1967 (Thu), former headquarters church. 
* This message was given on the first day of a gathering held before the second world tour (May 11 - June 9), after the testimonies of Lee Cho-nam and Min Kyung-sik, and has been organized from the notes taken by former association president Yoo Hyo-won and published in the June 1967 issue of <Seonghwa>. The title was added by the editor. 
344   Prayer and practice
To live a gracious life, one must sincerely and passionately pray for others. To become a prince of peace, one must become a person of heaven. 
The three years of public life were a period for Jesus to cultivate himself. The twelve disciples symbolize twelve types of humanity. To enter heaven, one must always pray and bear good fruit in interpersonal relationships. 
Even if one lived a life of devotion without going through the principle, it is false. To restore grace, one must pray and practice. Even if one could not pray, if they practice, they stand in the position of having prayed. If one prays once and practices ten times, they stand in the position of having prayed and practiced ten times. 
Words about the teacher must always be clarified and passed on. When the teacher is not present, horizontal connections must be made. One can only enter heaven through the twelve pearl gates. 
External blessings can be given. In the future, I plan to allow free marriages. At that time, one must stand in a position that can be a model in the eyes of God. 
Once three people align their hearts, they will not feel tired even without sleep. When there is no counterpart, the teacher speaks from the position of creating people. 
Until the teacher returns, I will work diligently, unite, and select 70 people to whom I will entrust responsibilities. On Saturday nights, we must hold an all-night vigil at the church. We must go on pilgrimage prayers daily, and while returning from pilgrimage prayers, we must witness to at least one person. If we cannot witness, we must bring back even those who used to come. 
The best way to evoke God's heart is to be sincere, so if three generations put their hearts together in sincerity, God will be with them, and their descendants will never fail. *
26)
God's providence at the end of days
<Summary of the message> In the end days, God will work centered on women. This is partly because women were the first to fall, but also because women symbolize the fallen land. 
Before the Unification Church emerged, there had to be a history of horizontal providence to complement the vertical providence. For over 40 years before the Lord appeared, the history of brides welcoming the groom had to manifest centered on women. In response, men also had to work to establish God's decisive center. All of these come through three stages. 
A woman called the wife of Jehovah must emerge to fulfill the restoration history. However, the person involved does not know this. In the process of the woman carrying out the indemnity restoration history, two-thirds is God's work, and one-third is Satan's work. This must be discerned. This should be handled purely with wisdom, a heart of loyalty and devotion, and a heart that seeks truth. 
That wife must be of the same age as the mother at the time of marriage (over 16 years old). Since she must testify, the teacher must initially serve her from the position of a servant. Otherwise, he cannot liberate the servant. This is similar to Jesus before John the Baptist. 
An adopted child must go through the position of the heavenly prime minister (referring to the loyal subject: one must go through the process of being a loyal subject to become an adopted child) to rise to the position of a direct son. After that, one must testify that they submit to the Lord. From that time, they will stand in a position where the Lord can govern them. If one complies, Satan will retreat; if one disbelieves, they will fall from that point. If one complies, the teacher will not suffer. 
Thus, a standard of indemnity restoration for Adam will be established. This providence of God has been testified to by older individuals. Therefore, a new mother will be welcomed. The teacher has come out of prison because the women prepared for this mission could not fulfill it. 
The teacher still has two things that are incomplete. You do not know this. Until now, I have established you as a reality to resolve the historical resentment of being offered as a sacrifice. Since there are still seven years left in the course, the standard of completion that the mother must reach remains. Therefore, in the headquarters, there can be no one who is not recognized by God, the teacher, and the members. When the teacher did not have a house, those who lived in houses are held accountable before God. The teacher has not been able to say everything he needs to say. 
In the end days, it will be a time filled with blessings, so many illnesses will arise. We are facing a significant historical turning point. Therefore, we must recall the time before entering the church and the time when we received grace and restart the seven-year course. Those who cannot restore the old standards must serve those who can. Thus, even if it means being carried by them, we must move forward. 
The teacher, being human, also has times of exhaustion. At those times, I think of the time when I was tortured in prison and return to the standard of establishing loyalty and devotion before heaven. 
When difficulties arise, if the teacher were to quit or rest, what would have happened to this path? What would have happened to God? 
To wake the sleeping and bless them, and to soothe the angry and bless them is God's greatest sorrow. In 1965, during my world tour, there was no joy. This was because countless heavenly children could not be connected. 
To allow each person to judge whether the path they are taking is true or not, the teacher feels the need to leave behind his history. In the end days, three women must emerge, with Kim Seong-do (Elder Jeong's mother) being the first, followed by Heo Ho-bin. * 
27)
The sincerity of the Heo Ho-bin faction
<Summary of the message> The second woman to emerge in preparing to welcome the Lord is Heo Ho-bin. 
Her husband is treated as a heavenly official in the position of Adam and must absolutely obey his wife. He must also serve alongside the Lord. For example, there were instances where he would bow to his wife 3,000 times. 
When the Lord came to this earth, he made enough clothes to change every three days throughout his life. 
On August 11, 1946, the teacher went to prison because of them and came out after three months. The teacher met them in prison, but they did not recognize him. The communists told the teacher's disciples, who were with him, that if they denied that the Lord came in the womb, they would be released from prison, but they insisted on it until the end and collapsed. One of those disciples had listened to the teacher's words, denied them, and came out. 
In the world, the twelve apostles are working, followed by the 72 families and the 120 families. 
When Heo was present, 1,200 people devoted themselves. Of these, 5 percent became sacrifices. 
The returning Lord must save them. What they did serves as a model for what we must do in the future, and the teacher must boast about their deeds to the world. 
In the future, those who will participate in the first resurrection must bow 7,000 times. If they do not reach that standard of sincerity, they will slander the Unification members. Compared to the standard of sincerity they offered for the returning Lord, the Unification members are severely lacking in sincerity. If they had fulfilled their mission at that time, the teacher would not have had to suffer. While the teacher was in prison, he spoke to her husband and disciples. 
Those who lead from the forefront can become miserable if they make mistakes. If the center is wrong, they will be slandered by Satan, and to indemnify this, God drives them to establish conditions of indemnity. This is why Jesus was also crucified. 
Indemnity is made horizontally centered on that one person. 
The teacher has set up three people in advance to observe their paths and determine the way forward based on heaven's judgment of them. This is wisdom. Therefore, one must always stand in a humble position. It is dangerous to put oneself first. Thus, one should not promote oneself but should stand in a position of being pursued and chased. 
If one undergoes ten trials, heaven will support them three times. This is because 8, 9, and 10 exceed the standard of indemnity over the 7,000-year history. Each person...
One must stand in the position of a Messiah to save one's own race. When one enters such a position, joy comes to each individual as their ancestors step forward to boast. When there is a mistake and a child is born, that mistake is inherited. How much would his ancestors lament when they see him resting before the final match? One must become a person who struggles to resolve God's resentment. When have we become the ones to establish conditions for the spirits to be resurrected and return? 

Now we must settle the past and welcome the new year of 1967. You must be more sincere than the prophets and ancestors.
